"[('', '625.')]","Her Iustus arcebiscop gehalgode Paulinum to biscope onxii kalendæ Augusti. Hic ciclus Dionisii quinque deconnouenalibus constans, hoc est xcv annis. sumitque exordium a xxx anno Incarnationis Domini, et desinit in dc xxvi anno. Hic ordo decennouenalis quem Græci Ennia kaið Iohannes papa Kaderida uocat, a Sanctis patribus in Nicea Sinodo fuit constitutus, in quo xiiii luna Paschalis omni anno sine ulla dubitatione." "[('', '626.')]",Her com Eomer fram Cwichelme West Seaxna cininge. þohte þæt he wolde ofstingan Eadwine cininge. ac he ofstang Lillan his ðegn. & Forðhere. & þone cining gewundode. "[('', '626.')]",& þære ilcan nihte wes Eadwine dohter acenned. seo wæs gehaten Eanfled. "[('', '626.')]",Þa gehet se cining Pauline þæt he wolde his dohter gesyllan Gode. gif he wolde abiddan æt Gode. þæt he moste his feonde afyllan. þe þone scaðan þider ær sende. "[('', '626.')]",& he þa for on West Seaxum mid fyrde. & afylde þærvciningas. & þæs folces mycel ofsloh. "[('', '626.')]",& Paulinus gefullade his dohter on Pentecosten twelfa sum. & se cining binnanxiimonað wæs gefullod on Eastrum mid eallum his dugoðe. þa wæron Estran onii idus Aprilis. "[('', '626.')]","Ðis wæs gedon on Eoferwic. þær he ær het getimbrian cyrican of treowe, seo wæs gehalgod on sancte Petres naman." La leof Sæxulf ic haue geseond æfter þe for mine saule þurfe. & ic hit wile þe wæl secgon for hwi. "[('', '656.')]","Min broðor Peada & min leoue freond Oswi ongunnen an mynstre Criste to loue & Sancte Petre. oc min broðer is faren of þisse liue swa swa Crist wolde. oc ic wile ðe gebidden la leoue freond þæt hii wirce æuostlice on þere werce. & ic þe wile finden þær to gold & siluer, land & ahte. & al þet þær to behofeð." "[('', '656.')]","Ða feorde se abbot ham & ongan to wircene, swa he spedde swa him Crist huðe. swa þet in feuna geare wæs þæt mynstre gare." "[('', '656.')]",& ic wile wurðigen þis dæi Crist & Sancte Peter. & ic wille þæt ge ealle getiðe mine worde. "[('', '656.')]",Ic Wulfere gife to dæi Sancte Petre & þone abbode Saxulf & þa munecas of þe mynstre þas landes & þas wateres & meres & fennes & weres & ealle þa landes þa þær abuton liggeð ða of mine kynerice sindon freolice. swa ðet nan man na haue þær nan onsting buton seo abbot & se muneces. "[('', '656.')]","Ðas is se gife: fram Medeshamstede to Norðburh, & to ðet stede þet man cleopeð Folies. & swa æl se feon riht to Esendic. & fra Esendic to þæt steode þe man cleopeð Feðermude. & swa þæt rihte weiexmile lang to Cuggedic. & swa to Raggewilh." "[('', '656.')]",& fra Raggewilh v mile to þe rihte æ þe gað to Ælm & to Wisebece. & swa abutan iii mile to Þrokonholt. & fra Þrokonholt riht þurh al ðe fen to Fereuorde þæt is xx mile lang. & swa to Grætecros. "[('', '656.')]",& fra Grætecros þurh an scyr wæter Bradan æ hatte. & þeononvimile to Paccelade. & swa forð þurh ælle þa meres & feonnes þa liggen toward Huntendune porte. Hit is litel þeos gife. ac ic wille þæt hi hit hælden swa kynelice & swa freolice. þæt þær ne benumen of na geld na gaule. buton to þa munecan ane. Agatho he wæs gehaten. & cydde him mid writ & mid worde. hu his breðre Peada & Wulfhere & se abbot Saxulf heafden wroht an minstre Medeshamstede wæs gehaten. & þæt hi hit heafden gefreod wið kyning & wið biscop of ealle þewdom. & bed him þæt he scolde þæt geten mid his writ & mid his bletsunge. "[('', '675.')]",And seo papa seonde þa his gewrite to Englalande þus cweðende. Ic Agatho papa of Rome grete wel seo wurðfulle æðelred Myrcene kyning & se ærcebiscop Theodorum of Cantwarbyrig. & seo Myrcene biscop Saxulf seo ær wæs abbot. & alle þa abbotes þa sindon on Englalande Godes gretinge & minre bletsunge. "[('', '675.')]",Ic haue geheord seo kyninges æðelredes geornunge & þes ærcebiscopes Theodorus. & þes biscopes Saxulfes. & þes abbotes Cuthbaldes. & ic hit wille þæt hit on ælle wise beo. swaswa ge hit sprecon hauen. "[('', '675.')]",And ic bebeode of Godes half & Sancte Petres. & ealra halgan. & ealre hadode heafde. þet ne kyning ne biscop ne eorl. ne nan man ne haue nan onsting. ne gafle ne geold ne feording ne nanes cinnes ðeudom ne nime man of þæt abbotrice of Medeshamstede. "[('', '675.')]",Ic beode æc þæt þe scyrbiscop ne seo swa dyrstlece þæt he ne hading ne haleging ne do on þis abbotrice buton seo abbot hit him bidde. ne biscopwite ne sinað ne nanes kinnes þing na haue þær nan onsting. "[('', '675.')]",& ic wille þæt seo abbot beo gehealden for legat of Rome ofer eal þæt iglande. & hwilc abbot þe beþ þær coren of þe munecan þæt he beo gebletsad of þan ærcebiscop of Cantwarbyrig. "[('', '675.')]","Ic wille & tyðe þæt whilc man swa haued behaten to faren to Rome, and he ne muge hit forðian. ouðer for untrumnisse, ouðer for lauerdes neode. ouðer for haueleste. ouðer for hwilces cinnes oðer neod he ne muge þær cumon. beo he of Englelande ouðer of hwilc oðer igland beo he. cume to þæt mynstre on Medeshamstede. & haue þæt ilce forgiuenesse of Criste & Sancte Peter. & of þonne abbot & of þone muneca þæt he scolde hauen gif he to Rome fore." "[('', '675.')]",Nu bidde ic þe broðer Theodorus þæt þu lete bedon geond æl Englelande þet seo sinað wurðe gegaderod. & þis write wurðe geredd & gehealdon. "[('', '675.')]",Alswa ic beode þe Saxulf biscop þæt swa swa þu hit geornest. þæt seo mynstre beo freo. swa ic forbeode þe & ealle þe biscopas þe æfter ðe cumon of Criste & of ealle his halgan þæt ge nan onsting ne hauen of þæt mynstre buton swa micel swa þone abbot wile. "[('', '675.')]",Nu wille ic hit segge mid worde þæt hwa swa halt þis write & þis bode. þa wurðe he efre wuniende mid God ælmihti on heuenrice. & hwa swa hit tobreceð. þa wurðe he amansumed & aniðrod mid Iudas & mid ealle deofle on helle buton he cume to dedbote. AMEN. "[('', '675.')]",Ðas writ seonde seo papa Agatho & an hundred & fif & twenti biscopes bi Wilfrid ærcebiscop of Eoferwic to Englalande. "[('', '675.')]",Þis wæs gedon æfter ure Drihtnes acennednessedc lxxxþes kiningesvigear æðelredes. "[('', '675.')]",Ða heot seo kining þone ærcebiscop Theodorus þæt he scolde setton ealle gewitenemot æt þone stede þæt man cleopeð Heatfelde. "[('', '675.')]",Ða hi wæron þær gegaderod. þa leot he rædon þa gewrite þe seo papa þider seonde. & ealle hit getton & fulfeostnodon. "[('', '675.')]","Ða seide se kyning, Ealle þa þing þe min broðer Peada. & min broðer Wulfere. & mine swuster Kineburh & Kynesuith geafon & getton Sancte Peter & þone abbot þa wile ic þæt stande. & ic wile on min dæi hit æcon for here sawle. & for minre sawle." "[('', '675.')]",Nu gife ic Sancte Peter todæi into his minstre Medeshamstede þas landes. & eal þæt þær to liggeð. þet is Bredune. Hrepingas. Cedenac. Swineshæfed. Heanbyrig. Lodeshac. Scuffanhalch. Costesford. Stretford. Wættelleburne. Lufgeard. Æþelhuniglond. Barþanig. "[('', '675.')]",Ðas landes ic gife Sancte Peter ealswa freolice swa ic seolf hit ahte. & swa þæt nan min æftergengles þær nan þing of ne nime. "[('', '675.')]",Gif hwa hit doð. þes papa curs of Rome & ealre biscope curs he habbe. & here ealre þe her be gewitnesse. & þis ic festnie mid Cristes tacne. "[('', '675.')]",Ic Theodorus ærcebiscop of Cantwarbyrig am witnesse of þas gewrite of Medeshamstede. & ic festnie mid min gewrite. & ic amansumie ealle þa þær aniþing ofbreke. & ic bletsie ealle þa þe hit healden. "[('', '675.')]",Ic Wilfrid ærcebiscop of Æferwic ic eam witnesse of þas gewrite. & ic gæte þæs ilce curs. "[('', '675.')]",Ic Saxulf þe wæs first abbot & nu eam biscop ic gife hi min curs & ealle min æftergengle þe þis tobreket. "[('', '675.')]",Ic Ostriðe æðelredes cwen hit tyðe. "[('', '675.')]",Ic Adrianus legat hit iete. "[('', '675.')]",Ic Putta biscop of Rofecestre ic hit write. "[('', '675.')]",Ic Waldhere biscop of Lundene hit festnie. "[('', '675.')]",Ic Cuðbald abbot hit geate swa þet hwa swa hit breket. ealre biscope cursunge & eal Cristene foces he hafe. Amen. "[('', '777.')]",Se ilca Beonne þurh ealle þa muneke red of þere minstre þa let he Cuðbriht xbondeland at Swines heafde mid læswe & mid mædwe. & mid eal þet ðær to læi. & swa þæt seo Cuðbriht geaf þone abboteLpunde þær fore. & ilca gear anes nihtes feorme ouðerxxxscyllinge penega. swa eac þæt eafter his dæi scolde seo land ongean in to þa mynstre. "[('', '777.')]",At þis gewitnesse wæs seo kining Offa. & seo kining Egferð. & seo ærcebiscop Hygeberht. & Ceolwulf biscop. & Inwona biscop. & Beonna abbot. & feola oþre biscopes & abbotes. & feola oðre rice men. "[('', '777.')]",On þes ilca Offa dæi. wæs an ealdorman Brordan wæs gehaten. he geornde at se kyning. þæt he scolde for his luuen freon his ane mynstre Wocingas het. for þi ðet he hit wolde giuen into Medeshamstede. & Sancte Peter. & þone abbote þe þa was. he was Pusa gehaten; "[('', '777.')]",Seo Pusa wæs æfter Beonna. and seo kining hine luuede swiðe. & seo kyning freode þa þæt mynstre Wocingas wið cining & wið biscop & wið eorl. & wið ealle men. swa þæt nan man ne hæfde þær nan onsting. buton Sancte Peter & þone abbod. "[('', '959.')]","On his dagum hit godode georne; & God him geuðe, þæt he wunode on sibbe, þa hwile þe he leofode, & he dyde, swa him þearf wes, earnode þes georne." "[('', '959.')]","He arerde Godes lof wide, & Godes lage lufode, & folces frið bette, swiðost þara cyninga, þe ær him gewurde, be manna gemynde." "[('', '959.')]","& God him eac fylste, þæt ciningas & eorlas georne him to bugon, & wurden underþeodde to þam þe he wolde, & butan gefeohte eal he gewilde, þet he sylf wolde." "[('', '959.')]","He wearð wide, geond þeodland, swiðe geweorðad, forþam þe he weorðode Godes naman georne, & Godes lage smeade, oft & gelome, & Godes lof rærde, wide & side, & wislice rædde, oftost a simle for Gode & for worulde, eall his þeode." "[('', '959.')]","Ane misdæda he dyde þeah to swiðe, þæt he ælþeodige unsida lufode & hæðene þeawas innan þysan lande gebrohte to fæste, & utlændisce hider in tihte, & deoriende leoda bespeon to þysan earde." "[('', '959.')]","Ac God him geunne, þæt his gode dæda swyðran wearðan þonne misdæda; his sawle to gescyldnesse on langsuman syðe." "[('', '963.')]",Her fram Eadgar cyning to ðe biscopdome on Wintanceastra wes gecoren Sancte Aðelwold. & þe arcebiscop of Cantwarbyrig Sancte Dunstan him gehalgod to biscop on þe fyrste sunnondæg of Aduent. þæt wæs oniii kalendæ Decembris. "[('', '963.')]","On þes oðer gear syþþon he wæs gehalgod. þa makode he feola minstra. & draf ut þa clerca of þe biscoprice, forþan þæt hi noldon nan regul healden. & sætta þær muneca." "[('', '963.')]",He macode þær twa abbotrice. an of muneca oðer of nunna. þæt wæs eall wiðinnan Wintanceastra. "[('', '963.')]","Syððan þa com he to se cyng Eadgar, bed him þet he scolde him giuen ealle þa minstre þa hæðene men hæfden ær to brocon. forði þet he hit wolde geeadnewion. & se kyng hit bliþelice tyðode." "[('', '963.')]","And se biscop com þa fyrst to Elig. þær Sancte Æðeldrið lið. & leot macen þone mynstre. geaf hit þa his an munac Brihtnoð wæs gehaten. halgode him þa abbot, & sætte þær munecas Gode to þewian. þær hwilon wæron nun. bohte þa feola cotlif æt se king. & macode hit swyðe rice." "[('', '963.')]","Syððon com se biscop Aðelwold to þære mynstre þe wæs gehaten Medeshamstede, ðe hwilon wæs fordon fra heðene folce. ne fand þær nan þing buton ealde weallas & wilde wuda." "[('', '963.')]","Fand þa hidde in þa ealde wealle writes þet Headda abbot heafde ær gewriton, hu Wulfhere kyng & æðelred his broðor hit heafden wroht. & hu hi hit freodon wið king, & wið biscop & wið ealle weoruldþeudom. & hu se papa Agatho hit feostnode mid his write. & se arcebiscop Deusdedit." "[('', '963.')]",Leot wircen þa þæt mynstre. & sætte þær abbot se wæs gehaten Aldulf. macede þær munecas þær ær ne wæs nan þing. "[('', '963.')]","Com þa to þe cyng, & leot him locon þa gewrite þe ær wæron gefunden." "[('', '963.')]","And se kyng andswerode þa & cwed. Ic Ædgar geate & gife todæi toforen Gode & toforen þone ærcebiscop Dunstan freodom Sancte Petres mynstre Medeshamstede of kyng, & of biscop. & ealle þa þorpes þe ðærto lin. þæt is Æstfeld. & Dodesthorp. & Ege. & Pastun." "[('', '963.')]","& swa ic hit freo þet nan biscop ne haue þær nane hæse, buton se abbot of þone minstre." "[('', '963.')]","And ic gife þone tun þe man cleopað Vndela, mid eall þet þær to lið, þæt is þet man cleopeð Eahte hundred. & market & toll, swa freolice þæt ne king ne biscop ne eorl ne ne haue þær nane hæse. ne nan man buton se abbot ane, & þam þe he þærto sæt." "[('', '963.')]","And ic gife Crist & Sancte Peter, & þurh þes biscop bene Aðelwold. þas land. þæt is Barwe. Wermigtun. Æsctun. Ketering. Castra. Egleswurðe. Waltun. Wiðringtun. Ege. "[('', '963.')]",And ic wille þæt markete beo in þe selue tun. & þæt nan oþer ne betwix Stanford & Huntandune. & ic wille þet þus be gifen se toll. fyrst fra Witlesmære eall to þe cinges toll of Norðmannes cros hundred. & eft ongeanward fra Witlesmære þurh Merelade on an to Nen. & swa swa þæt wæter reonneð to Crulande. & fra Crulande to Must. & fra Must to Cynges dælf & to Witlesmære. "[('', '1006.')]","& þa ofer þone midne sumor com þa se Denisca flota to Sandwic. & dydon eall swa hi ær gewuna wæron, hergodon & bærndon. & slogon swa swa hi ferdon." "[('', '1006.')]",Þa het se cyng abannan ut ealne ðeodscipe of Westseaxum. & of Myrcean. & hi lagon ute þa ealne þone herfest on fyrdinge ongean þone here. ac hit naht ne beheold þe ma þe hit oftor ær dyde. "[('', '1006.')]",Ac for eallum þissum se here ferde swa he sylf wolde. & se fyrdinge dyde þære landleode ælcne hearm. þet him naðor ne dohte ne innhere ne uthere. "[('', '1006.')]",Ða hit winter leohte. þa ferde se fyrd ham. "[('', '1006.')]",& se here com þa ofer Martinus messan to his fryðstole to Wihtlande. & tilode him þær æghwer þæs ðe hi behofdan. "[('', '1006.')]","& þa to ðam middan wintran eodon heom to heora garwan feorme ut þurh Hamtunscire into Barrucscire to Rædingan. and hi dydon heora gewuna, atendon heora beacna swa swa hi ferdon." "[('', '1006.')]",& ferdon þa to Wealingaforda. & þet eall forsweldon. & wændon him þa andlang Æscesdune to Cwicelmes hlæwe. "[('', '1006.')]",& þær onbidedon beotra gylpa. forþon oft man cwæð. gif hi Cwicchelmes hlæwe gesohton. þet hi næfre to sæ gan ne sceoldan. wendon þa oðres wæges hamweard. "[('', '1006.')]","Þa wæs þær fyrd gesomnod æt Cynetan. & hi þær togædere fengon. & sona þet wærod on fleame gebrohtan, & syððan hyra herehuðe to sæ færedon." "[('', '1006.')]",Þær mihton geseon Winceastre leodan rancne here. & unearhne. þæt hi be hyra gate to sæ eodon. & mæte & madmas oferLmila him fram sæ fættan. "[('', '1006.')]",Þa wæs se cyng gewend ofer Temese into Scrobbesbyrigscire. & nam þær his feorme in þære middewintres tide. "[('', '1006.')]",Þa wearð hit swa mycel æge fram þam here. þet man ne mihte geþeoncean ne asmægian hu man of earde hi gebringon sceolde. oððe þisne eard wið hi gehealdan. forþan þe hi hæfdon ælce scire on West Sexum stiðe gemarcod mid bryne. & mid hergunge. "[('', '1006.')]",Agan se cyng georne to smeagenne wið his witan hwet heom eallum rædlicost þuhte. þæt man þisum earde gebeorgan mihte ær he mid ealle fordon wurðe. "[('', '1006.')]",Ða gerædde seo cyng & his witan eallum þeodscipe to þearfe. þeah hit him eallum lað wære. þæt man nyde moste þam gafol gyldan. "[('', '1006.')]",Ða sende se cyng to þam here. & him cyþan het þæt he wolde þæt heom grið betweonan beon sceolde. & him man gafol and metsunge syllan sceolde. & hi ða ealle þæt underfengon. & him man geond Angelcyn. "[('', '1007.')]",Her on ðissum geare wæs þet gafol gelæst þam unfriðe here. þæt wæsxxxþusend punda. "[('', '1007.')]",& On ðissum geare eac wæs Ædric gesett to ealdorman on Myrcena rice. "[('', '1008.')]",Her bebead se cyng þæt man sceolde ofer eall Angelcynn scipu feastlice wircean. þæt is þonne þrym hund hidum. & ofxhidon ænne scegð. & ofviiihidum helm & byrnan. "[('', '1009.')]",Her on þissum geare gewurdon þa scipu gearwe þe we ær ymbe spræcon. & heora wæs swa feala swa næfre ær þes ðe us bec secgað on Angelcynne ne gewurdon on nanes cynges dæg. "[('', '1009.')]",& hi man þa ealle togædere ferode to Sandwic. & þær sceoldan licgan. & þisne eard healdan wið ælcne uthere. ac we gyt næfdon þa geselða. ne þone wurðscipe þæt seo scipfyrd nytt wære ðisum earde. þe ma þe heo oftor ær wæs. "[('', '1009.')]",Ða gewearð hit on þisum ilcan timan oððe litle ær þet Brihtric Eadrices broðor ealdormannes forwregde Wulfnoð cild þone Suðseaxscian to þam cyning. "[('', '1009.')]",& he þa utgewende. & him þa to aspeon þet he heafdexxscipa. & he þa hergode æghwer be ðam suðriman. & ælc yfel wrohton. "[('', '1009.')]",Ða genam se Brihtric him to hundeahtatig scipa. & þohte þæt he him myceles wordes wircean sceolde. þæt he Wulfnoð cuconne oððe deadne begytan sceolde. "[('', '1009.')]",Ac þa hi þyderweard wæron. þa com him swilc wind ongean swilce nan mann ær ne gemunde. & þa scipo ða ealle tobeot. & toþræsc. & on land wearp. & com se Wulfnoð sona. & ða scipo forbærnde. "[('', '1009.')]",Ða þis cuð wæs to ðam oðrum scipon þær se cyng wæs hu ða oðre geferdon. wæs þa swilc hit eall rædleas wære. & ferde se cyng him ham. & þa ealdormenn. & þa heahwitan. & forleton þa scipo þus leohtlice. "[('', '1009.')]",& þet folc þa þe on ðam scipe wæron færcodon ða scipo eft to Lundene. & leton ealles ðeodscipes geswincg þus leohtlice forwurðan. & næs se ege na betera þe eall Angelcynn tohopode. "[('', '1009.')]",Þa ðeos scipfyrd ðus geendod wæs. þa com sona æfter hlammessan se ungemetlica unfriðhere to Sandwic. & sona wendon heora fore to Cantwarbyrig. & þa burh raðe geeodon. gif hi þe raðor to him friðes to ne girndon. "[('', '1009.')]",Þa het se cyng abannan ut ealne þeodscipe þet mann on ælce healfe wið hi gehealden sceolde. ac þeah hweðere hi ferdon loc hu hi woldon. "[('', '1009.')]",Þa sum siðe heafde se cyng hi forebegan mid ealre fyrde. þa hi to scipan woldon. & eall folc gearu wæs heom on to fonne. ac hit wæs ða þurh Eadric ealdorman gelet swa hit þa æfre wæs. "[('', '1009.')]",Ða æfter sanctus Martinus mæssan. þa ferdon hi eft ongean to Cent. & namon him wintersettl on Temesan. & lifedon of East Seaxum. & of ðam scirum þe þær nyxt wæron on twam healfe Temese. & oft hi on þa burh Lundene gefuhton. "[('', '1009.')]",Ac si Gode lof. þet heo gyt gesund stent. & hi þær æfre yfel geferdon. "[('', '1009.')]","Þa gewarnode man hi þæt þær wæs fyrd æt Lundene ongean. hi gewendon þa ofer æt Stane. & þus ferdon ealne þone winter, & ðone lencten wæron him on Cent. and bettan heora scipa." "[('', '1011.')]",Her on þissum geare sende se cyng & his witan to ðam here. & georndon friðes. & him gafol & metsunga behetan. wið þam þe hi heora hergunga geswicon. "[('', '1011.')]",Hi heafdon þa ofergan East Englaiand East Seaxeii& Middel Seaxeiii& Oxenafordscireiiii& Grantabrycgescirev& Heortfordscirevi& Bucingahamscirevii& Bedanfordscireviii& healfe Huntadunscirex& be suðan Temese ealle Centingas. & Suð Seaxe. & Hæstingas. & Suðrig. & Bearrucscire. & Hamtunscire. & micel on Wiltunscire. "[('', '1015.')]",Ða gaderode Eadric ealdorman fyrde & se æðeling Eadmund be norðan. "[('', '1015.')]",Ða hi togædere comon. þa wolde se ealdorman beswicon þone æþeling. & hi tohwurfon þa buton gefeohte forþam. & rimdon heora feondum. "[('', '1015.')]",& Eadric ealdormann aspeon þaxlscipa fram þam cyning. & beah þa to Cnute. "[('', '1015.')]",& West Seaxe bugon & gislodon. & horsodon þone here. & he wæs þær þa oð midne winter. "[('', '1016.')]",Her on þissum geare com Cnut cyning mid his hereclxscipa. & Eadirc ealdormann mid him ofer Temese into Myrcan æt Cræcilade. "[('', '1016.')]",& wendon þa to Wæringscire innon þære middewintres tide. & hergodon & bærndon & slogon eall þæt hi to comon. "[('', '1016.')]",Ða ongan se æðeling Eadmund to gadrienne fyrde. "[('', '1016.')]",Þa fyrd gesomnod wæs. þa ne onhagode him buton se cyng þære wære. & hi hæfdon þære burhware fultum of Lundene. "[('', '1016.')]",Geswicon þa þære fyrding. & færde ælc mann him ham. "[('', '1016.')]",Ða æfter þære tide þa bead mann eft fyrde be fullum wite. þæt ælc mann þe feor wære forð gewende. "[('', '1016.')]",& mann sende to þam cyninge to Lundene. & bædon hine þæt he come ongean þa fyrde mid þam fultume þe he gegaderian mihte. "[('', '1016.')]",Ða hi ealle tosomne comon. þa ne beheold hit naht þe ma þe hit oftor ær dyde. "[('', '1016.')]",Þa cydde mann þam cyninge þæt hine mann beswicon wolde. þa þe him on fultume beon sceolden. Forlet ða þa fyrde. & cyrde him eft to Lundene. "[('', '1016.')]",Ða rad se æþeling Eadmund to Norðhymbran to Vhtrede eorl. & wænde ælc mann þæt hi woldon fyrde somnian ongean Cnut cyng. "[('', '1016.')]",Þa ferdon hi into Stæffordscire. & into Scrobbesbyrig. & to Legeceastre. "[('', '1016.')]",& hergodon hi on heora healfe & Cnut on his. "[('', '1016.')]",& wende him þa ut þurh Buccingahamscire into Beadafordscire. & þanon to Huntandunscire. andlang fennes to Stanforda. & ða into Lincolnescire. þanon to Snotingahamscire. & swa to Norðhymbran to Eoforwicweard. "[('', '1016.')]",Ða Uhtred geaxode þis. ða forlet he his hergunga & efeste norðweard. & beah þa for nede. & ealle Norðhymbran mid him. "[('', '1016.')]",& he gislode. & hine man ðeah hwæðere ofsloh. & þurcytel Nafanan sunu mid him. "[('', '1016.')]",& þa æfter þæs se cyng Cnut gesætte Yric into Norðhymbran to eorle. eall swa Uhtred wæs. "[('', '1016.')]",& syððan wendon him suðweard oðres weges eall be westan. & com þa eall se here toforan þam Eastron to scipon. "[('', '1016.')]",& se æþeling Ædmund wende to Lundene to his fæder. & þa æfter Eastron wende se cyng Cnut mid eallum his scipum to Lundeneweard. "[('', '1016.')]",Ða gelamp hit þet se cyng æðelred forðferde ær ða scipu comon. "[('', '1016.')]",He geendode his dagas on sanctes Georius mæssedæge æfter mycclum geswince. & earfoðnissum his lifes. "[('', '1016.')]",& þa æfter his ende. ealle þa witan þe on Lundene wæron & se burhwaru gecuron Eadmund to cynge. & his rice he heardlice werode þa hwile þe his tima wæs. "[('', '1016.')]",Þa comon þa scipo to Grenawic to þam gandagum. & binnon lytlum fæce wendon to Lundene. "[('', '1016.')]",& dulfon þa ane mycele dic on ða suðhealfe & drogon heora scipa on westhealfe þære brycge. & bedicodon syððon þa burh uton þæt nan mann ne mihte ne inn ne ut. "[('', '1016.')]",& oft rædlice on ða burh fuhton. ac hi heom heardlice wiðstodon. "[('', '1016.')]",Þa wæs Eadmund cyng ær þam gewend ut. & gerad þa West Seaxan. & him beah eall folc to. "[('', '1016.')]",& raðe æfter þam he gefeaht wið þone here æt Peonnan wið Gillinga. & oðer gefeoht he gefeaht æfter middan sumera æt Sceortstane. "[('', '1016.')]",Se here gewende þa æfter þam fram Lundene mid heora scipum into Arwan. & þar up foran. & feordon on Myrcean. & slogon & bærndon swa hwæt swa hi oferforon. swa heora gewuna wæs. "[('', '1016.')]",& heom metes tilodon. & hi drifon ægðer ge scipa. ge heora drafa into Medewæge. "[('', '1016.')]",Ða gesomnode Eadmund cyngiiiisiþe ealle Englaþeode. & ferde ofer Temese to Brentforda. & ferde innan Cent. "[('', '1016.')]",Se here gewende eft up on East Seaxan. & ferde into Myrcean. & fordydon eall þæt he oferferde. "[('', '1016.')]",Ða se cyng geaxode þæt se here uppe wæs. ða gesomnode hevsiðe ealle Englaþeode. & ferde him æt hindan. & offerde hi innan East Seaxan æt þere dune þe mann hæt Assandun. & þær togædere heardlice fengon. "[('', '1016.')]",Ða dyde Eadric ealdormann swa he oftor ær dyde. astealde þone fleam ærest mid Magesæton. & swa aswac his cynehlaforde. & ealle þeode. "[('', '1016.')]",& þa cyningas comon togædere æt Olanige. & heora freondscipe þær gefæstnodon. ge mid wedde ge mid aðe. & þæt gyld setton wið þone here. "[('', '1022.')]",& he syððan mid þam pallium þær mæssode swa se papa him gewissode. & he hine gereordode æfter þam mid þam papan. & syððon mid fulre bletsunge ham gewende. "[('', '1046.')]",& behet man him þæt he moste wurðe ælc þæra þinga þe he ær ahte. "[('', '1046.')]","Ða wiðlæg Harold eorl his broðor & Beorn eorl, þæt he ne moste beon nan þæra þinga wurðe þe se cyng him geunnen hæfde. ac sette man himiiiinihta grið to his þæt scipon." "[('', '1046.')]",Ða wearð hit under þam þet þam cynge com word unnfrið scipa lægen bewestan and hergodon. "[('', '1046.')]",Ða Godwine eorl west onbuton mid þes cyngesiiscipum. þam anan steorde Harold eorl. & þam oðran Tostig his broðor. & landesmanna scipaxlii. "[('', '1046.')]",Þa scyfte man Harold eorl up þæs cynges scipe þe Harold eorl ær steorde. þa gewendon hi west to Peuenesea. & lægen þær wederfeste. "[('', '1046.')]",Þa þes binnoniidagum. þa com Swegen eorl þider. & spec wið his feder & wið Beorn eorl. & bed Beorn þæt he sceolde faran mid him to ðam cynge to Sandwic. & fylstan him to þæs cynges freondscipe. & he þæs tiðode. "[('', '1046.')]",Gewendon heom þa swylce hi woldon to ðam cynge. "[('', '1046.')]",Ða amang þam þe hi ridon. þa bæd Swegen hine þet he sceolde faran mid him to his scipon. tealde þæt his sciperes woldon wændon fram him buton he þe raðor come. "[('', '1046.')]",Hi gewendon þa begen þær his scipu lægen. "[('', '1046.')]",Þa hi þyder comon. þa bæd Swegen eorl hine þæt he sceolde gewendon mid him to scipe. "[('', '1046.')]",He forweornde swiðe. swa lange oð his sciperes gefengon hine. & wurpon hine on þone bat. & bundon hine. & reowan to scipe. & dydon hine þær on. "[('', '1046.')]",Tugon þa up heora segel. & urnon west to Axamuðan. & hæfdon hine mid heom. oð þet hi ofslogon hine. & namon þone lichaman. & bebyrgedon innan anre cyrican. "[('', '1046.')]",& comon þa his freond & litsmen of Lundene. & namon hine up. & feredon hine to Winceastre to Ealdanmynstre. & he is þær byrged wið Cnut cyng his eam. "[('', '1046.')]",& Swegen gewende þa east to Baldewineslande. & sæt þær ealne winter on Brycge mid his fullan griðe. "[('', '1046.')]",& on þam ylcan geare forðferde Eadnoð biscop benorðan. & sette man Ulf to biscop. "[('', '1047.')]",Her on þisum geare wæs mycel gemot on Lundene to midfestene. & man sette utixlitsmanna scipa. & fif belifan wið æftan. "[('', '1047.')]",& on þysum ilcan geare com Swegen eorl into Englalande. "[('', '1047.')]",& on þysum ilcan geare wæs se mycele sinoð on Rome. & Eadward cyng sende þider Hereman biscop. & Ealdred biscop. & hi comon þyder on Easteræfen. "[('', '1047.')]","& eft se papa hæfde sinoð on Uercel. & Vlf biscop com þærto. & forneah man sceolde tobrecan his stef, gif he ne sealde þe mare gersuman. forðan he ne cuðe don his gerihte swa wel swa he sceolde." "[('', '1047.')]",& on þisum geare forðferde Eadsige arcebiscopiiii kalendæ Novembris. "[('', '1048.')]",Her on þisum geare Eadward cyng gesette Rodbyrd on Lundene to arcebiscop to Cantwarabyrig on Lengtene. & þæs sylfan Lentenes he for to Rome æfter his pallium. "[('', '1048.')]",& se cyng geaf þet biscoprice on Lundene Sparhafoc abbot of Abbandune. & se cyng geaf <þæt> abbotrice Roðulfe biscop his mæge. "[('', '1048.')]",Ða com se fram Rome ane dæge ær sanctus Petrus mæsseæfene. & gesæt his æt Cristescyrcean on sanctus Petrus mæssedæg. & sona þæs to þam cyng gewænde. "[('', '1048.')]",Ða com Sparhafoc abbod be to him mid þæs cynges gewrite & insegle. to þan þet he hine hadian sceolde to biscop into Lundene. þa wiðcweð se arcebiscop. & cwæð þet se papa hit him forboden hæfde. "[('', '1048.')]","Þa gewende se abbod ongean þone arcebiscop eft to ðam, & þær þes biscophades gernde. & se arcebiscop him anrædlice forwernde. & cwæð þet se papa hit him forboden hæfde." "[('', '1048.')]",Ða gewende se abbod to Lundene. & sæt on þam biscoprice þe se cyng him ær geunnan hæfde be his fulre leafe ealne þone sumor & þone hærfest. "[('', '1048.')]",& com þa Eustatius fram geondan sæ sona æfter þam biscop. & gewende to ðam cynge. & spæc wið hine þæt þæt he þa wolde. & gewende þa hamweard. "[('', '1048.')]",Þa he com to Cantwarbyrig east þa snædde he þær & his menn. & to Dofran gewende. "[('', '1048.')]",Ða he wæs sume mila oððe mare beheonan Dofran. þa dyde he on his byrnan. & his geferan ealle. & foran to Dofran. "[('', '1048.')]",Þa hi þider comon. þa woldon hi innian hi þær heom sylfan gelicode. "[('', '1048.')]",Þa com an his manna. & wolde wician æt anes bundan huse his unðances. & gewundode þone husbundon. & se husbunda ofsloh þone oðerne. "[('', '1048.')]",Ða wearð Eustatius uppon his horse. & his gefeoran uppon heora & ferdon to þam husbundon. & ofslogon hine binnan his agenan heorðæ. "[('', '1048.')]",& wendon him þa up to þære burgeweard. & ofslogon ægðer ge wiðinnan ge wiðutan. ma þannexxmanna. & þa burhmen ofslogonxixmenn on oðre healfe. & gewundoden þæt hi nystan hu fela. "[('', '1048.')]",& Eustatius ætbærst mid feawum mannum. & gewende ongean to þam cynge. & cydde be dæle hu hi gefaren hæfdon. "[('', '1048.')]",& wearð se cyng swiþe gram wið þa burhware. & ofsænde se cyng Godwine eorl. & bæd hine faran into Cent mid unfriða to Dofran. forþan Eustatius hæfde gecydd þam cynge þet hit sceolde beon mare gylt þære burhwaru þonne his. "[('', '1048.')]",Ac hit næs na swa. & se eorl nolde na geðwærian þære infare. forþan him wæs lað to amyrrene his agenne folgað. "[('', '1048.')]",Ða sende se cyng æfter eallon his witan. & bead heom cuman to Gleaweceastre neh þære æftre sancte Maria mæssan. "[('', '1048.')]",Þa hæfdon þa welisce menn gewroht ænne castel on Herefordscire on Swegenes eorles folgoðe. & wrohten ælc þæra harme. & bismere þæs cynges mannan þær abutan þe hi mihton. "[('', '1048.')]",Ða com Godwine eorl & Swegen eorl & Harold eorl togædere æt Byferesstane. & manig mann mid heom. to ðon þæt hi woldon faran to heora cynehlaforde. & to þam witan eallon þe mid him gegaderode wæron. þæt hi þæs cynges ræd hæfdon & his fultum. & ealra witena. hu hi mihton þæs cynges bismer awrecan & ealles þeodscipes. "[('', '1048.')]",Ða wæron þa wælisce men ætforan mid þam cynge. & forwregdon ða eorlas. þet hi ne moston cuman on his eagon gesihðe. Forðan hi sædon þæt hi woldon cuman þider for þes cynges swicdome. "[('', '1048.')]",Wæs þær cuman Siward eorl & Leofric eorl. & mycel folc mid heom norþan to þam cynge. & wæs þam eorle Godwine & his sunan gecydd þæt se cyng & þa menn þe mid him wæron. woldon rædon on hi. & hi trymedon hi fæstlice ongean. þæh him lað wære þæt hi ongean heora cynehlaford standan sceoldan. "[('', '1048.')]",Ða gerædden þa witan on ægðer halfe þæt man ða ælces yfeles geswac. & geaf se cyng Godes grið & his fulne freondscipe on ægðre healfe. "[('', '1048.')]",Ða gerædde se cyning & his witan þæt man sceolde oðre syðan habban ealra gewitena gemot on Lundene to hærfestes emnihte. "[('', '1048.')]",& het se cyning bannan ut here. ægðer ge besuðan Temese ge benorðan eall þæt æfre betst wæs. "[('', '1048.')]",Ða cwæð man Swegen eorl utlah. & stefnode man Godwine eorle & Harolde eorle to þon gemote swa raðe swa hi hit gefaran mihton. "[('', '1048.')]",Þa hi þider utcomon. þa stefnede heom man to gemote. þa gyrnde he griðes & gisla. þet he moste unswican into gemote cuman. & ut of gemote. "[('', '1048.')]",Ða gyrnde se cyng ealra þæra þegna þe þa eorlas ær hæfdon. & hi letan hi ealle him to handa. "[('', '1048.')]",Þa sende se cyng eft to heom. & bead heom þæt hi comon midxiimannum into þæs cynges ræde. "[('', '1048.')]",Þa geornde se eorl eft griðes & gisla. þæt he moste hine betellan æt ælc þæra þinga þe him man on lede. "[('', '1048.')]",Þa wyrnde him mann ðera gisla. & sceawede him mannvnihta grið ut of lande tofarenne. "[('', '1048.')]",& gewende þa Godwine eorl & Swegen eorl to Bosenham & scufon ut heora scipu. & gewendon heom begeondan sæ. & gesohton Baldewines grið. & wunodon þær ealne þone winter. "[('', '1048.')]",& Harold eorl gewende west to Yrlande. & wæs þær ealne þone winter on þes cynges griðe. "[('', '1048.')]",& sona þæs þe þis wæs. þa forlet se cyng þa hlæfdian. seo wæs gehalgod him to cwene. & let niman of hire eall þæt heo ahte. on lande. & on golde. & on seolfre & on eallon þingon. & betæhte hy his swyster to Hwerwillon. "[('', '1048.')]",& Sparhafoc abbod wearð ða adrifen ut of þam biscoprice on Lundene. & wes Willelm þæs cynges preost gehadod þærto. "[('', '1048.')]",& man sette þa Oddan to eorle ofer Defenascire. & ofer Sumersæton. & ofer Dorseton. & ofer Wealas. & mann sette Ælfgar Leofrices sunu eorles ðane eorldom on handa þe Harold ær ahte. "[('', '1052.')]",Her on ðisum geare forðferde Ælfgiue Ymma Eadwardes cynges modor & Hardacnutes cynges. "[('', '1052.')]",& on þam sylfan geare gerædde se cyng & his witan þæt mann sceolde forðian ut to Sandwic scipu. & setton Raulf eorl & Oddan eorl to heafodmannum þærto. "[('', '1052.')]",Ða gewende Godwine eorl ut fram Brycge mid his scypum to Yseran. and let ut ane dæge ær midsumeres mæsseæfene þæt he com to Næsse. þe is besuðan Rumenea. "[('', '1052.')]",Þa com hit to witenne þam eorlum ut to Sandwic. & hi þa gewendon ut æfter þam oðrum scipum. & bead man landfyrde ut ongean þa scipu. "[('', '1052.')]",Þa amang þison þa wearð Godwine eorl gewarnod. & gewende him þa into Pefenesea. & wearð þæt wæder swiðe strang. þæt þa eorlas ne mihton gewitan hwet Godwine eorl gefaren hæfde. "[('', '1052.')]",& gewende þa Godwine eorl ut agean þæt he com eft to Brycge. & ða oðra scipu gewenden heom eft ongean to Sandwic. "[('', '1052.')]",& gerædde man þa þæt þa scipu gewendan eft ongean to Lundene. & sceolde man setton oðre eorlas & oðre hasæton to þam scipum. ða lengde hit man swa lange þæt seo scipfyrd eall belaf. & gewendon ealle heom ham. "[('', '1052.')]",Ða geaxode Godwine eorl þet. & teah þa up his segl & his lið. & gewendon heom þa west on an to Wiht. & eodon þær up. & hergodon swa lange þær þæt þæt folc geald heom swa mycel swa hi heom on legden. "[('', '1052.')]",& gewendon heom þa westweard oð þet hi comon to Portlande. & eodon þær up & dydon to hearme swa hwet swa hi don mihton. "[('', '1052.')]",Þa wes Harold gewend ut of Yrlande mid nigon scipon. & com þa up æt Portlocan. & wes þær mycel folc gegaderod ongean. ac he ne wandode na him metes to tylienne. "[('', '1052.')]",Eode up. & ofsloh þær mycelne ende þes folces. & nam him on orfe. & on mannum. & on æhtum. swa him gewearð. "[('', '1052.')]",& gewende him þa eastweard to his feder. & gewendon heom þa begen eastweard þæt hi comon to Wiht. & namon þær þæt him ær wiðæftan wæs. "[('', '1052.')]",& gewendon heom þa þanon to Pefenesea. & begeat forð mid him swa fela scipu. swa þær fera wæron. & swa forð þæt he com to Næsse. & begeat ealle þa scipu. þe wæron on Rumenea. & on Hyþe & on Folcesstane. "[('', '1052.')]",& gewendon þa east to Dofran. & eodon þær up. & namon him þær scipu. & gislas. swa fela swa hi woldon. "[('', '1052.')]",& ferdon swa to Sandwic. & dydon hand þæt sylfa. & heom man geaf æghwer gislas. & metsunga. þær þær hi gyrndon. "[('', '1052.')]",& gewendon heom þa to Norðmuðan. & swa to Lundeneweard. "[('', '1052.')]",& sume þa scipu gewendon binnon Scepige. & dydon þær mycelne hearm. & gewendon heom to Middeltune þæs cynges. & forbearndon þæt eall. & wæron heom to Lundeneweard æfter þam eorlan. "[('', '1052.')]",Þa hi to Lundene comon. þa læg se cyng & þa eorlas ealle þær ongean midLscipum. "[('', '1052.')]",Þa sendon þa eorlas to þam cynge. & gerndon to him þæt hi moston beon wurðe ælc þæra þinga þe heom mid unrihte ofgenumen wæs. "[('', '1052.')]",Ða wiðlæg se cyng sume hwile þeah. swa lange oð þet folc þe mid þam eorle wes. wearð swiðe astyred ongean þone cyng. & ongean his folc. swa þæt se eorl sylf earfoðlice gestylde þæt folc. "[('', '1052.')]",Þa ferde Stigand biscop to mid Godes fultume. & þa wise menn ægðær ge binnan burh ge buton. & geræddon þæt man tremede gislas on ægðer healfe. & man swa dyde. "[('', '1052.')]",Ða geaxode Rotberd arcebiscop & þa Frencisce menn þæt. genamon heora hors. & gewendon sume west to Pentecostes castele. sume norð to Rodbertes castele. "[('', '1052.')]",& Rodberd arcebiscop & Vlf biscop gewendon ut æt Æstgeate. & heora geferan. & ofslogon. & elles amyrdon manige iunge men. "[('', '1052.')]",& gewendon heom on an to Ealdulfesnæse. & wearð him þær on anon unwræste scipe. & ferde him on an ofer sæ. & forlet his pallium Cristendom ealne her on lande. swa swa hit God wolde. þa he ær begeat þone wurðscipe swa swa hit God nolde. "[('', '1052.')]",Ða cwæð mann mycel gemot wiðutan Lundene. & ealle þa eorlas & þa betstan menn þe wæron on þison lande wæron on þam gemote. "[('', '1052.')]",Þær bær Godwine eorl up his mal. & betealde hine þær wið Eadward cyng his hlaford & wið ealle landleodan. þet he wæs unscyldig þæs þe him geled wæs. & on Harold his sunu. & ealle his bearn. "[('', '1052.')]",& se cyng forgeaf þam eorle & his bearnum his fulne freondscype & fulne eorldom & eall þet he ær ahte. & eallon þam mannon þe him mide wæron. & se cyng geaf þære hlæfdian eall þæt heo ær ahte. "[('', '1052.')]","& cweð man utlaga Rotberd arcebiscop fullice, & ealle þa Frencisce menn. forðan þe hi macodon mæst þet unseht betweonan Godwine eorle & þam cynge." "[('', '1052.')]",& Stigand feng to þam on Cantwarabyrig. "[('', '1052.')]",& On þis ilcan tyme forlet Arnwi abbod of Burh abbotrice. be his halre life. & geaf hit Leofric munec be þes cynges leafe & þære munece. & se abbot Arnwi lifode syððonviiiwintre. "[('', '1052.')]",& se abbot þa þæt mynstre swa þæt man hit cleopede þa Gildeneburh. þa wæx hit on land & on gold & on seolfer. "[('', '1053.')]",Her on þisum geare forðferde Godwine eorl onxvii kalendæ Mai. & he is bebyrged on Winceastre. on Ealdanmynstre. & feng Harold eorl his sunu to ðam eorldome. & to eallum þam þe his fæder ahte. & feng Ælfgar eorl to ðam eorldom þe ær ahte. "[('', '1054.')]",Bellum apud mare mortuum. "[('', '1054.')]",Her on þisum geare forðferde Leo se halga papa on Rome. "[('', '1054.')]",& on þisum geare wæs swa mycel orfcwealm. swa man ne gemunde fela wintrum ær. "[('', '1054.')]",& Uictor wæs gecoren to papan. "[('', '1055.')]",Her on þisum geare forðferde Siward eorl. "[('', '1055.')]",& þa bead man ealre witenagemotviinihton ær mid lenctene. & utlagode mann Ælfgar eorl. forðon him man wearp on. þæt he wæs þes cynges swica. & ealra landleoda. "[('', '1055.')]",& he þæs geanwyrde wes ætforan eallum þam mannum þe þær gegaderode wæron. þeah him þæt word ofscute his unnþances. "[('', '1056.')]",.hic Henricus Romanorum imperator obiit. cui successit filius eius Henricus. "[('', '1057.')]",Her on þisum geare com Ædward æðeling Eadmundes sunu cynges hider to lande. & sona þæs gefor. & his lic is bebyrged innon sanctus Paulus mynstre on Lundene. "[('', '1057.')]",& Victor papa forðferde. & wæs Stephanus gecoren to papan. se wæs abbot on Monte Cassiono. "[('', '1058.')]",& on þisum geare forðferde Heaca biscop on Suð Seaxan. & Stigand arcebiscop hadode Ægelric æt Cristes cyrcean to biscop to Suð Seaxum. & Siward abbot to biscop to Hrofeceastre. "[('', '1059.')]",Her on þisum geare wæs Nicolaus to papan gecoren. se wæs biscop æt Florentie þære burh. & wæs Benedictus utadrifen se wæs ær papa. "[('', '1060.')]",Hic Henricus rex Francorum obiit. cui successit Phylippus filius eius. "[('', '1060.')]",On þissum geare forðferde Kynsige arcebiscop on Eoforwic onxi kalendæ Ianuarii. & feng Ealdred biscop þærto. & Walter feng to þam biscoprice on Hereforda. "[('', '1061.')]",Her on þisum geare forðferde Duduc biscop on Sumersæton. & feng Gisa to. "[('', '1061.')]",And on þam ilcan geare forðferde Godwine biscop æt Sancte Martine onvii Idus Marcii. "[('', '1061.')]",And on þam sylfan geare forðferde Wulfric abbod æt sancte Augustine innon þære Easter wucan onxiiii kalendæ Mai. "[('', '1061.')]",Ða com þam cynge word þæt se abbod Wulfric forðgefaren wæs. þa geceas he Æðelsige munuc þærto of Ealdon mynstre. folgode þa Stigande arcebiscop. & wearð gehalgod to abbod æt Windlesoran. on sanctus Augustinus mæssedæg. "[('', '1062.')]",Hoc anno subiuguta est Cynomannia comiti Normanniæ Willelmo. "[('', '1063.')]",Her for Harold eorl & his broðor Tostig eorl. ægðer ge mid landfyrde ge mid sciphere into Brytlande. & þet land geeodon. & þæt folc heom gislodon & to bugon. "[('', '1063.')]",& foron syððan to & ofslogon heora cyng Griffin. & brohton Harolde his heafod. & he sette oþerne cyng þærto. "[('', '1064.')]",Her on þisum geare foron Norðhymbra togædere. & utlagodon heora eorl Tostig. & ofslogon his hiredmenn ealle þa hi mihton tocuman ægðer ge Englisce ge Dænisce. "[('', '1064.')]",& namon ealle his wepna on Eoferwic. & gol & seolfor. & ealle his sceattas þe hi mihton ahwar þær geaxian. "[('', '1064.')]",& senden æfter Morkere Ælfgares sune eorles. & gecuron hine heom to eorle. "[('', '1064.')]",& he for suð mid eallre þære scire. & mid Snotinghamscire. & Deorbiscire. & Lincolnascire. oð he com to Hamtune. & his broðor Eadwine him com togeanes mid þam mannum þe on his eorldome wæron. & eac fela Bryttas comon mid him. "[('', '1064.')]",Ðær com Harold eorl heom togeanes. & hi lægdon ærende on hine to þam cynge Eadwarde. & eac ærendracan mid him sendon. & bædon þæt hi moston habban Morkere heom eorle. "[('', '1064.')]",& se cyng þæs geuðe. & sende eft Harolde heom to Hamtune. on sancte Simones & Iudan mæsseæfen. & kydde heom þæt ilce. & heom þet on hand sealdon. & he niwade þær Cnutes lage. "[('', '1064.')]","& þa norðerne men dydan mycelne hearme abutan Hamtune. þa hwile þe he for on heora ærende. ægðer þæt hi ofslogon men. & bærndon hus and cornn. & namon eall þet orf þe hi mihton tocuman. þæt wæs fela þusend, & fela hund manna hi namon." "[('', '1064.')]",& læddon norð mid heom. swa þet seo scyre & þa oðra scyre þe þær neh sindon. wurdon fela wintra þe wyrsan. "[('', '1064.')]",& Tostig eorl. and his wif & ealle þa þe woldon þæt he wolde. foron suð ofer sæ mid him to Baldewine eorle. & he hig ealle underfeng. & hi wæron ealne þone winter þær. "[('', '1066.')]",On þissum geare man halgode þet mynster æt Westmynster on Cildamæssedæg. "[('', '1066.')]",& se cyng Eadward forðferde on twelfta mæsse æfen. & hine mann bebyrgede on twelftan mæssedæg. innan þære niwan halgodre circean on Westmynstre. "[('', '1066.')]",& Harold eorl feng to Englalandes cynerice. swa swa se cyng hit him geuðe. & eac men hine þær togecuron. & wæs gebletsod to cynge on twelftan mæssedæg. "[('', '1066.')]",& þy ilcan geare þe he cyng wæs. he for ut mid sciphere togeanes Willelme. "[('', '1066.')]",& þa hwile com Tostig. eorl into Humbran midlxscipum. Eadwine eorl com landfyrde. & draf hine ut. & þa butse carlas hine forsocan. "[('', '1066.')]",& he for to Scotlande midxiisnaccum. & hine gemette Harold se Norrena cyng midcccscipum. & Tostig him tobeah. "[('', '1066.')]",& hi bægen foran into Humbran. oð þet hi coman to Eoferwic. & heom wiðfeaht Morkere eorl. & Eadwine eorl. & se Norrena cyng ahte siges geweald. "[('', '1066.')]",& man cydde Harolde cyng hu hit wæs þær gedon & geworden. & he com mid mycclum here Engliscra manna. & gemette hine æt Stængfordes brycge. & hine ofsloh. & þone eorl Tostig. & eallne þone here ahtlice ofercom. "[('', '1066.')]",& þa hwile com Willelm eorl upp æt Hestingan on sancte Michaeles mæssedæg. & Harold com norðan & him wiðfeaht ear þan þe his here come eall. & þær he feoll. & his twægen gebroðra Gyrð & Leofwine. "[('', '1066.')]",& Willelm þis land geeode. & com to Westmynstre. & Ealdred arcebiscop hine to cynge gehalgode. & menn guldon him gyld. & gislas sealdon. & syððan heora land bohtan. "[('', '1066.')]",& ða wæs Leofric abbot of Burh æt þæt ilca feord. & sæclode þær & com ham. & wæs dæd sone þær æfter on ælre halgan mæsseniht. "[('', '1066.')]",God are his saule. "[('', '1066.')]",On his dæg wæs ealle blisse & ealle gode on Burh. & he wæs leaf eall folc. swa þæt se cyng geaf sancte Peter & him þæt abbotrice on Byrtune. & se of Couentre þæt se eorl Leofric þe wæs his eam ær heafde macod. & se of Crulande. & se of þorneie. "[('', '1066.')]",& he dyde swa mycel to gode into þæt mynstre of Burh on golde & on seolfre & on scrud & on lande. swa nefre nan oðre ne dyde toforen him ne nan æfter him. "[('', '1066.')]",Þa wearð gildene burh to wrecce burh. "[('', '1066.')]",Ða cusen þa munecas to abbot Brand prouost. forðan þæt he wæs swiðe god man & swiðe wis. & senden him þa to Ædgar æðeling. forðan þet þe landfolc wendon þæt he sceolde cyng wurðen. & se æðeling hit him geatte þa bliþolice. "[('', '1066.')]",Þa þe cyng Willelm geherde þæt secgen. þa wearð he swiðe wrað. & sæde þæt se abbot him heafde forsegon. "[('', '1066.')]",Þa eodon gode men heom betwenen & sahtloden heom forðan þæt se abbot wæs goddera manne. "[('', '1066.')]",Geaf þa þone cyngxlmarc goldes to sahtnysse. & þa lifede he litle hwile þær æfter buton þry gear. "[('', '1066.')]",Syððon comen ealle dræuednysse & ealle ifele to þone mynstre. "[('', '1066.')]",God his gemyltse. "[('', '1067.')]",Her for se cyng ofer sæ. & hæfde mid him gislas & sceattas. "[('', '1067.')]",& com þæs oðres geares on sancte Nicolaes mæssedæg. & þæs dæges forbearn Cristes cyrce on Cantwarabyrig. "[('', '1067.')]",& he geaf ælces mannes land þa he ongean com. "[('', '1067.')]",& þæs sumeres for Eadgar cild ut. & Mærle swegen. & fela manna mid heom. & foran to Scotlande. & se cyng Melcolm hi ealle underfeng. & genam þes cildes swuster to wife Margaretan. "[('', '1068.')]",Her on þissum geare Willelm cyng geaf Rodberde eorle þone eorldom on Norðhymbraland. "[('', '1068.')]",Ða comon þa landesmenn togeanes him. & hine ofslogon. &ixhund manna mid him. "[('', '1068.')]",And Eadgar æðeling com þa mid eallum Norðhymbram to Eoferwic. & þa portmen wið hine griðedon. "[('', '1068.')]",& se cyng Willelm suðan mid eallan his fyrde. & þa burh forhergode. & fela hund manna ofsloh. & se æðeling for eft to Scotlande. "[('', '1069.')]",Her man wrægde þone biscop Ægelric on Burh. & sende hine to Westmynstre. & utlagode his broðer Ægelwine biscop. "[('', '1069.')]",Þa betwyx þam twam sancta Marian mæssan. comon easton of Dænmarcun midcccscipum. þæt wæron Swægnes sunan cynges. & his broðer Osbearn eorl. "[('', '1069.')]",& þa ferde se eorl Walðeaf ut. & com he & Eadgar æðeling. & fela hund manna mid heom. & gemetton þet lið innan Humbran. "[('', '1069.')]",& ferdon to Eoferwic. & upp eodan & þa castelas gewunnan. & ofslogon fela hund manna. & to scipe læddon sceattas fela. & þa heafodmen hæfdon on beandon. & lagon betwyx Vsan & Trentan ealne þone winter. "[('', '1069.')]",& se cyng Willelm for into þære scire. & hi eall . "[('', '1069.')]",& on þisum ilcan geare forðferde Brand abbod of Burh. onv kalendæ Decembris. "[('', '1070.')]",Her se eorl Walþeof griðede wið þone cyng. & þæs on lengten se cyng let hergian ealle þa mynstra þe on Englalande wæron. "[('', '1070.')]",Þa on þam ilcan geare com Swegn cyng of Denmarcan into Humbran. & þæt landfolc comen him ongean & griðedon wið hine wændon þæt he sceolde þet land ofergan. "[('', '1070.')]",Þa comen into Elig þa Densce biscop & Osbearn eorl & þa Densca huscarles mid heom. "[('', '1070.')]",& þet Englisce folc of eall þa feonlandes comen to heom. wendon þæt hi sceoldon winnon eall þæt land. "[('', '1070.')]","Þa herdon þa munecas of Burh sægen þæt heora agene menn wolden hergon þone mynstre, þæt wæs Hereward & his genge." "[('', '1070.')]",Þæt wæs forðan þet hi herdon sæcgen þet se cyng heafde gifen þæt abbotrice an Frencisce abbot Turolde wæs gehaten. & þæt he wæs swiðe styrne man. & wæs cumen þa into Stanforde mid ealle hise Frencisce menn. "[('', '1070.')]",Þa wæs þære an cyrceweard Yware wæs gehaten. nam þa be nihte eall þet he mihte. þet wæron Cristes bec & mæssehakeles & cantelcapas & reafes & swilce litles hwat. swa hwat swa he mihte. "[('', '1070.')]",& ferde sona ær dæg to þone abbot Turolde & sægde him þæt he sohte his griðe. & cydde him hu þa utlages sceolden cumen to Burh. þæt he dyde eall be þære munece ræde. "[('', '1070.')]","Þa sona on morgen comen ealle þa utlaga mid fela scipe, & woldon into þam mynstre. & þa munecas wiðstoden þæt hi na mihton incumen." "[('', '1070.')]",Þa lægdon hi fyr on. & forbærndon ealle þa munece huses & eall þa tun buton ane huse. "[('', '1070.')]","Þa comen hi þurh fyre in æt Bolhiðe geate. & þa munecas comen heom togeanes. beaden heom grið, ac hi na rohten na þing." "[('', '1070.')]",Geodon into þe mynstre. clumben upp to þe halge rode. namen þa þe kynehelm of ure Drihtnes heafod eall of smeate golde. namen þa þet fotspure þe wæs undernæðen his fote. þæt wæs eall of read golde. "[('', '1070.')]",Clumben upp to þe stepel. brohton dune þæt hæcce þe þær wæs behid. hit wæs eall of gold & of seolfre. hi namen þære twa gildene scrines &ixseolferne. "[('', '1070.')]",& hi namen fiftene mycele roden. ge of golde ge of seolfre. "[('', '1070.')]",Hi namen þære swa mycele gold & seolfre & swa manega gersumas on sceat & on scrud & on bokes swa nan man ne mæi oðer tællen. sægdon þæt hi hit dyden for ðes mynstres holdscipe. "[('', '1070.')]","Syððon geden heom to scipe. ferden heom to Elig, betæhtan þær þa ealla þa gærsume;" "[('', '1070.')]",Þa Denescæ menn wændon þæt hi sceoldon ofercumen þa Frencisca men. þa todrefodon ealle þa munekes. beleaf þær nan butan an munec he wæs gehaten Leofwine lange. he læi seoc in þa secræman in. "[('', '1070.')]",Ða com Turold abbot & æhte siþe twenti Frencisce men mid him & ealle fullwepnode. "[('', '1070.')]",Þa he þider com þa fand he forbærnd wiðinnan & wiðutan. eall butan þa cyrece ane. "[('', '1070.')]",Þa wæron þa utlagas ealle on flote. wistan þæt he scolde þider cumen. "[('', '1070.')]",Þis wæs don þæs dægesiiii Nonæ Iunii. "[('', '1070.')]",Þa twegen kyngas Willelm & Swægn wurðon sæhtlod. þa ferdon þa Dænesca menn ut of Elig mid ealle þa forenspræcena gærsume & læddon mid heom. "[('', '1070.')]",Þa hi comen on middewarde þe sæ. þa com an mycel storm & todræfede ealle þa scipe þær þa gersumes wæron inne. sume ferdon to Norwæge. sume to Yrlande. sume to Dænmarce. "[('', '1070.')]",& eall þæt þider com þæt wæs þone hæcce & sume scrine & sume roden & fela of þa oðre gærsume. & brohten hit to an cynges tun hatte. & dyden hit eall þa in þone cyrce. "[('', '1070.')]",Ða syððon þurh heora gemelest & þurh heora druncenhed on an niht forbærnde þa cyrce. & eall þet þær innæ wæs. "[('', '1070.')]",Ðus wæs se mynstre of Burch forbærnd & forhærgod. "[('', '1070.')]",Ælmihtig God hit gemiltse þurh his mycele mildhertnesse. "[('', '1070.')]",And þus se abbot Turolde com to Burh. & þa munecas comen þa ongean. & dydan Cristes þeudom in þære cyrce. þæt ær hæfde standen fulle seofeniht forutan ælces cynnes riht. "[('', '1070.')]",Ða herde Ægelric biscop þet gesecgon. þa amansumede he ealle þa men þa þæt yfel dæde hæfden don. "[('', '1070.')]",Ða wæs mycel hunger þæs geares. "[('', '1070.')]",& þa þæs sumeres com þet lið norðan of Humbran into Tæmese. & lagon þær twa niht. & heoldan syððon to Dænmercan. "[('', '1070.')]",And Baldewine eorl forðferde. & his sunu Arnulf feng to rice. "[('', '1070.')]",& Willelm eorl sceolde ben his geheald. & Franca cyng eac. & com þa Rodbriht eorl & ofsloh his mæg Arnulf. & þone eorl. & þone cyng aflymda. and his menn ofsloh fela þusenda. "[('', '1071.')]",Her Ædwine eorl & Morkere eorl uthlupon & mislice ferdon on wudu & on felda. "[('', '1071.')]",Ða gewende Morkere eorl to Elig on scipe. And Eadwine eorl wearð ofslagen arhlice fram his agenum mannum. "[('', '1071.')]",& com se biscop Egelwine. & Siward Bearn. & fela hund manna mid heom into Elig. "[('', '1071.')]",& þa þe se cyng Willelm þæt geaxode. þa bead he ut scipfyrde & landfyrde. & þet land abutan sæt. & brycge gewrohte. & inn for. & seo scipfyrde on þa sæhealfe. "[('', '1071.')]",& þa utlagan þa ealle on hand eodan. þæt wæs Egelwine biscop. & Morkere eorl. & ealle þa þe mid heom wæron buton Herewarde ane. "[('', '1071.')]",& ealle þa þe mid him woldon. & he hi ahtlice utlædde. "[('', '1071.')]",& se cyng genam scipa & wæpna & sceattas manega. & þa men he ateah swa swa he wolde. & þone biscop Egelwine he sende to Abbandune. & he þær forðferde sona þæs wintres. "[('', '1072.')]",Her Willelm cyng lædde scipfyrde & landfyrde to Scotlande. & þæt land on þa sæhealfe mid scipum ymbelæg. & his landfyrde æt þam Gewæde innlædde. & he þær naht ne funde þæs þe him þe bet wære. "[('', '1072.')]",& se cyng Melcolm com & griðede wið þone cyng Willelm & gislas sealde. & his man wæs. "[('', '1072.')]",& se cyng ham gewende mid ealre his fyrde. "[('', '1072.')]",& se biscop Egelric forðferde. he wæs to biscop hadod to Eoferwic. ac hit wæs mid unrihte him ofgenumon. "[('', '1072.')]",& man geaf him þæt biscoprice on Dunholme. & he heafde hit þa hwile þe he wolde. & forlet hit syððan. & ferde to Burch to sancte Petres mynstre. & þær drohtnodexiigear. "[('', '1072.')]",Ða æfter þam þe Willelm cyng gewan Englalande. þa nam he hine of Burch & sende hine to Westmynstre. "[('', '1072.')]",& he forðferde onIDus Octobris. & he is bebyrged þær innan þam mynstre. innon sanctus Nicolaus portice. "[('', '1073.')]",On þisum geare Willelm cyng lædde Engliscne here & Frencisce ofer sæ. & gewan þæt land Mans. "[('', '1073.')]",& hit Englisce men swyðe amyrdon. wingearðas hi fordydon. & burga forbærndon. & swiðe þet land amyrdon. & hit eall abegdon Willelme to handa. "[('', '1073.')]",& hi syððon ham gewendon to Englalande. "[('', '1074.')]",On þisum geare for Willelm cyng ofer sæ to Normandig. & Eadgar cild com of Scotland to Normandige. "[('', '1074.')]",& se cyng hine geinlagode. & ealle his men. & he wæs on þes cynges hyrede. & nam swilce gerihta swa se cyng him geuðe. "[('', '1075.')]",On þisum geare Willelm cyng geaf Raulfe eorle Willelmes dohtor Osbearnes sunu. & se ylca Raulf wæs Bryttisc on his moderhealfe. & his fæder wæs Englisc Raulf hatte. & wæs geboren on Norðfolc. "[('', '1075.')]",Þa geaf se cyng his sunu þone eorldom on Norðfolc. & Suðfolc. þa lædde he þæt wif to Norðwic. "[('', '1075.')]",Þær wes þæt brydeala mannum to beala. "[('', '1075.')]",Ðær wæs Roger eorl. & Walþeof eorl. & biscopas & abbotes. & ræddon þær swa þæt hi woldon þone cyng gesettan ut of Englelandes cynedome. "[('', '1075.')]",& hit wearð sona gecydd þam cynge to Normandige hu hit wæs geræd. þæt wæs Roger eorl. & Raulf eorl. þe wæron yldast to ðam unreode. & hi speonan þa Bryttas heom to. & sendon east to Denmearcan æfter sciphere heom to fultume. "[('', '1075.')]",& Roger ferde west to his eorldome. & gegaderode his folc to þæs cynges unþearfe. ac he wearð gelet. "[('', '1075.')]",& Raulf eac on his eorldome wolde forðgan mid his folce. ac þa castelmen þe wæron on Englalande & eac þæt landfolc him togeanes comen. & gemacodon þæt he naht ne dyde. ac for to scipe æt Norðwic. "[('', '1075.')]",& his wif wæs innan þam castele. & hine heold swa lange þæt man hire grið sealde. & heo ut ferde þa of Englalande. & ealle hire men þe hire mid woldon. "[('', '1075.')]",& se cyng siððan com to Englalande. & genam Roger eorl his mæg. & gefestnode hine. & Walþeof eorl he genam eac. "[('', '1075.')]",& Eadgið seo hlæfdig forðferde on Winceastreviinihton ær Cristes mæssan. & se cyng hi let bryngan to Westmynstre mid mycclan wurðscipe. & lægde hi wið Eadward kyng hire hlaforde. "[('', '1075.')]",& se wæs on Westmynstre þone midewinter. & man fordyde þær ealle þa Bryttas þe wæron æt þam brydealoð æt Norðwic. "[('', '1076.')]",On þisum geare forðferde Swægn cyng on Dænmercan. & Harold his sunu feng to þe kynerice.
