"[('', '1076.')]",& se cyng for ofer sæ. & lædde his fyrde to Brytlande. & beset þone castel Dol. "[('', '1076.')]",& þa Bryttas hine heoldon þæt se cyng com of Francland. & Willelm þanon for. & þær forleas ægðer ge men ge hors. & feola his gersuma. "[('', '1077.')]",Her on þisum geare wurdon sæhte Franca cyng & Willelm Englalandes cyng. ac hit heold litle hwile. "[('', '1077.')]",& ðes geares forbarn Lundenburh anre nihte ær Assumptio sancte Mariæ swa swyðe swa heo næfre ær næs syðþan heo gestabeled wæs. "[('', '1077.')]",And on þisum geare forðfyrde Ægelwig abbod on Euesham on þam dægexiv kalendæ Marcii. And Hereman biscop eac forðferde on þam dægex kalendæ Marcii. "[('', '1079.')]",On þisum geare com Melcolm cyng of Scotlande into Englelande betwyx þam twam Mariam mæssan mid mycclum fyrde. & gehergode Norðhymbraland oð hit com to Tine. & ofsloh feala hund manna. & ham lædde manige sceattas. & gersuma. & menn on heftninge. "[('', '1079.')]",And þi ilcan geare se cyng Willelm gefeaht togeanes his sunu Rotbearde wiðutan Normandige be anum castele Gerborneð hatte. & se cyng Willelm wearð þær gewundod. & his hors ofslagen þe he on sæt. & eac his sunu Willelm wearð þær gewundod. & fela manna ofslagene. "[('', '1080.')]",On þisum geare wæs se biscop Walchere ofslagen on Dunholme æt anum gemote. & an hund manna mid him Frencisce & Flemisce. & he sylf wæs on Hloðeringa geboren. þis dydon Norðhymbran on Maies monðe. "[('', '1081.')]",ON þisum geare se cyng lædde fyrde into Wealan. & þær gefreode fela hund manna. "[('', '1082.')]",Her nam se cyng Odan biscop. & her wæs mycel hungor. "[('', '1083.')]",On þisum geare aras seo ungehwærnes on Glæstingabyrig betwyx þam abbode Þurstane. & his munecan. "[('', '1083.')]",Ærest hit com of þæs abbotes unwisdome. þæt he misbead his munecan on fela þingan. "[('', '1083.')]",& ða munecas hit mændon lufelice to him. & beadon hine þæt he sceolde healdan hi rihtlice. & lufian hi. & hi woldon him beon holde. & gehyrsume. "[('', '1083.')]",Ac se abbot nolde þæs naht. ac dyde heom yfele. & beheot heom wyrs. "[('', '1083.')]",Anes dæges þe abbot eode into capitulan. & spræc uppon þa munecas. & wolde hi mistukian. "[('', '1083.')]",& sende æfter læwede mannum. & hi comon into capitulan on uppon þa munecas full gewepnede. & þa wæron þa munecas swiðe aferede of heom. nyston hwet heom to donne wære. "[('', '1083.')]",Ac to scuton. sume urnon into cyrcean. & belucan þa duran into heom. & hi ferdon æfter heom into þam mynstre. & woldon hit utdragan. þaða hig ne dorsten na utgan. "[('', '1083.')]",Ac reowlic þing þær gelamp on dæg. þæt þa Frencisce men bræcen þone chor & torfedon towærd þam weofode þær ða munecas wæron. & sume of ðam cnihtan ferdon uppon þone uppflore. & scotedon adunweard mid arewan toweard þam haligdome. swa þæt on þære rode þe stod bufon þam weofode sticodon on mænige arewan. "[('', '1083.')]",& þa wreccan munecas lagon onbuton þam weofode. & sume crupon under. & gyrne cleopedon to Gode his miltse biddende. þa þa hi ne mihton nane miltse æt mannum begytan. "[('', '1083.')]",Hwæt magon we secgean. buton þæt hi scotedon swiðe. & þa oðre ða dura bræcon þær adune & eodon inn. "[('', '1083.')]",& ofslogon sume þa munecas to deaðe. & mænige gewundedon þærinne. swa þæt ðet blod com of ðam weofode uppon þam gradan. & of ðam gradan on þa flore. "[('', '1083.')]",Þreo þær wæron ofslagene to deaðe. & eahteteone gewundade. "[('', '1083.')]",& on þæs ilcan geares forðferde Mahtild Willelmes cynges cwen. on þone dæg æfter ealra halgena mæssedæg. "[('', '1083.')]",And on þes ylcan geares æfter midewintre se cyng let beodan mycel gyld & hefelic ofer eall Englaland. þæt wæs æt ælcere hyde twa & hund seofenti peanega. "[('', '1084.')]",Her on ðisum geare forðferde Wulfuuold abbod on Ceortesege. on þam dægexiii kalendæ Mai. "[('', '1085.')]",On þisum geare menn cwydodon & to soðan sædan. þæt Cnut cyng of Denmearcan Swægnes sune cynges fundade hiderward. & wolde gewinnan þis land mid Rodbeardes eorles fultume of Flandran. forðan þe Cnut heafde Rodbeardes dohter. "[('', '1085.')]",Ða Willelm Englalandes cyng þe þa wæs sittende on Normandige. forðig he ahte ægðer ge Englaland ge Normandige. þis geaxode. he ferde into Englalande mid swa mycclan here ridendra manna. & gangendra of Francrice and of Brytlande. swa næfre ær þis land ne gesohte. swa þæt menn wundredon hu þis land mihte eall þone here afedan. "[('', '1085.')]",Ac se cyng let toscyfton þone here geond eall þis land to his mannon. & hi fæddon þone here ælc be his landefne. "[('', '1085.')]",& men heafdon mycel geswinc þæs geares. & se cyng lett awestan þæt land abutan þa sæ. þet gif his feond comen upp. þæt hi næfdon na on hwam hi fengon swa rædlice. "[('', '1085.')]",Ac þa se cyng geaxode to soðan þæt his feond gelætte wæron. & ne mihten na geforðian heora fare. þa lett he sum þone here faren to heora agene lande. & sum he heold on þisum lande ofer winter. "[('', '1085.')]",Ða to þam midewintre wæs se cyng on Gleaweceastre mid his witan. & heold þær his hiredvdagas. & syððan þe arcebiscop & gehadode men hæfden sinoð þreo dagas. "[('', '1085.')]",Ðær wæs Mauricius gecoren to biscop on Lundene. & Willelm to Norðfolce & Rodbeard to Ceasterscire. hi wæron ealle þæs cynges clerecas. "[('', '1085.')]",Æfter þisum hæfde se cyng mycel geþeaht. & swiðe deope spæce wið his witan ymbe þis land hu hit wære gesett. oððe mid hwylcon mannon. "[('', '1085.')]",Sende þa ofer eall Englaland into ælcere scire his men. & lett agan ut hu fela hundred hyda wæron innon þære scire. oððe hwet se cyng him sylf hæfde landes. & orfes innan þam lande. oððe hwilce gerihtæ he ahte to habbanne toxiimonþum of ðære scire. "[('', '1085.')]",Eac he lett gewritan hu mycel landes his arcebiscops hæfdon. & his leodbiscops. & his abbods. & his eorlas. & þeah ic hit lengre telle. hwæt oððe hu mycel ælc mann hæfde þe landsittende wæs innan Englalande. on lande. oððe on orfe. & hu mycel feos hit wære wurð. "[('', '1085.')]","Swa swyðe nearwelice he hit lett ut aspyrian. þæt næs an ælpig hide. ne an gyrde landes. ne furðon, hit is sceame to tellanne. ac hit ne þuhte him nan sceame to donne. an oxe. ne an cu. ne an swin. næs belyfon. þæt næs gesæt on his gewrite." "[('', '1085.')]",& ealle þa gewrita wæron gebroht to him syððan. "[('', '1085.')]",Her se cyng bær his corona & heold his hired on Winceastre to þam Eastran. & swa he ferde þæt he wæs to þam Pentecosten æt Wæstminstre. & dubbade his sunu Henric to ridere þær. "[('', '1085.')]",Syððan he ferde abutan swa þæt he com to Lammæssan to Searebyrig. & þær him comon to his witan. and ealle þa landsittende men. þe ahtes wæron ofer eall Engleland. wæron þæs mannes men þe hi wæron. "[('', '1085.')]",& ealle hi bugon to him. & weron his menn. & him holdaðas sworon þæt hi woldon ongean ealle oðre men him holde beon. "[('', '1085.')]",Ðanon he ferde into Wiht. forþig he wolde faran into Normandige & swa dyde syððan. "[('', '1085.')]",And þeah he dyde ærest æfter his gewunan. begeat swiðe mycelne sceatt of his mannan þær he mihte ænige teale tohabban oððe mid rihte oððe elles. "[('', '1085.')]",Ferde þa syððan into Normandige. & Eadgar Æþeling Ædwardes mæg cynges beah þa fram him forþig he næfde na mycelne wurðscipe of him. ac se ælmihtiga God him gife wurðscipe on þam toweardan. "[('', '1085.')]",& Cristina þæs æðelinges swuster beah into mynstre to Rumesege. & underfeng halig rest. "[('', '1085.')]",& þæs ilcan geares wæs swiðe hefelic gear. & swiðe swincfull & sorhfull gear innan Englelande on orfcwealme. & corn. & wæstmas wæron ætstandene. "[('', '1085.')]",& swa mycel ungelimp on wæderunge. swa man naht æðelice geþencean ne mæg. swa stor þunring. & lægt wes. swa þæt hit acwealde manige men. & aa hit wyrsode mid mannan swiðor & swiðor. "[('', '1085.')]",GEbete hit God elmihtiga. þonne his willa sy. "[('', '1086.')]",Æfter ure Drihtnes Hælendes Cristes gebyrtide. an þusend wintra & seofan & hundeahtatig wintra. on þam an & twentigan geare þæs þe Willelm weolde & stihte Engleland swa him God uðe. gewearð swiðe hefelic and swiðe woldberendlic gear on þissum lande. "[('', '1086.')]",Swylc coðe com on mannum. þæt fullneah æfre þe oðer man wearð on þam wyrrestan yfele. þet is on ðam drife. & þet swa stranglice. þæt mænige menn swulton on ðam yfele. "[('', '1086.')]",Syððan com þurh þa mycclan ungewiderunge þe comon swa we beforan tealdon. swyðe mycel hungor ofer eall Engleland. þæt manig hundred manna earmlice deaðe swulton þurh þone hungor. "[('', '1086.')]",Eala hu earmlice & hu reowlic tid wæs ða. "[('', '1086.')]",Ða ða wreccæ men lægen fordrifene fullneah to deaðe. & syððan com se scearpa hungor & adyde hi mid ealle. "[('', '1086.')]",Hwam ne mæg earmian swylcere tide? "[('', '1086.')]",Oððe hwa is swa heardheort þæt ne mæg wepan swylces ungelimpes? "[('', '1086.')]",Ac swylce þing gewurðaþ for folces synna þæt hi nellað lufian God & rihtwisnesse. "[('', '1086.')]",Swa swa hit wæs þa on ðam dagum. þæt litel rihtwisnesse wæs on þisum lande mid ænige menn. buton mid munecan ane þær þær hi wæll ferdon. "[('', '1086.')]",Se cyng & þa heafod men lufedon swiðe & oferswiðe gitsunge. on golde. & on seolfre. & ne rohtan hu synlice hit wære begytan buton hit come to heom. "[('', '1086.')]",Se cyng sealde his land swa deore to male. swa heo deorost mihte. "[('', '1086.')]",Ðonne com sum oðer & bead mare þonne þe oðer ær sealde. & se cyng hit lett þam menn þe him mare bead. "[('', '1086.')]",Ðonne com se þridde. & bead geat mare. & se cyng hit let þam men to handa þe him eallra meast bead. & ne rohte na hu swiðe synlice þa gerefan hit begeatan of earme mannon. ne hu manige unlaga hi dydon. "[('', '1086.')]",Ac swa man swyðor spæc embe rihte lage. swa mann dyde mare unlaga. "[('', '1086.')]",Hy arerdon unrihte tollas. & manige oðre unriht hi dydan. þe sindon earfeþe to areccenne. "[('', '1086.')]",Eac on ðam ilcan geare ætforan hærfeste forbarn þæt halige mynster sancte Paule þe biscopstol on Lundene. & mænige oðre mynstres. & þæt mæste dæl & þæt rotteste ealle þære burh. "[('', '1086.')]",Swylce eac on ðam ilcan timan forbarn fullneah ælc heafodport on eallon Englalande. "[('', '1086.')]",Eala reowlic & wependlic tid wæs þæs geares. þe swa manig ungelimp wæs forðbringende. "[('', '1086.')]",Eac on þam ilcan geare toforan Assumptio sancte Marie for Willelm cyng of Normandige into France mid fyrde. & hergode uppan his agenne hlaford Philippe þam cynge. "[('', '1086.')]",& sloh of his mannon mycelne dæl. & forbearnde þa burh Maðante. & ealle þa halige mynstres þe wæron innon þære burh. & twegen halige menn þe hyrsumedon Gode on ancersettle wuniende. þær wæron forbearnde. "[('', '1086.')]",Ðissum þus gedone. se cyng Willelm cearde ongean to Normandige. "[('', '1086.')]",Reowlic þing he dyde. & reowlicor him gelamp. "[('', '1086.')]",Hu reowlicor? "[('', '1086.')]",Him geyfelade. & þæt him stranglice eglade. "[('', '1086.')]",Hwæt mæg ic teollan? "[('', '1086.')]",Se scearpa deað þe ne forlet ne rice menn. ne heane. seo hine genam. "[('', '1086.')]",He swealt on Normandige on þone nextan dæg æfter natiuitas sancte Marie. & man bebyrgede hine on Caþum æt sancte Stephanes mynstre. ærer he hit arærde. & syððan mænifealdlice gegodade. "[('', '1086.')]",Eala hu leas & hu unwrest is þysses middaneardes wela. "[('', '1086.')]",Se þe wæs ærur rice cyng. & maniges landes hlaford. he næfde þa ealles landes buton seofon fot mæl. & se þe wæs hwilon gescrid mid golde. & mid gimmum. he læg þa oferwrogen mid moldan. "[('', '1086.')]",He læfde æfter him þreo sunan. Rodbeard het se yldesta. se wæs eorl on Normandige æfter him. se oðer het Willelm. þe bær æfter him on Engleland þone kinehelm. Se þridda het Heanric. þam se fæder becwæð gersuman unateallendlice. "[('', '1086.')]",Gif hwa gewilnigeð to gewitane hu gedon mann he wæs. oððe hwilcne wurðscipe he hæfde. oððe hu fela lande he wære hlaford. ðonne wille we be him awritan swa swa we hine ageaton. ðe him on locodan. & oðre hwile on his hirede wunedon. "[('', '1086.')]",Se cyng Willelm þe we embe specað wæs swiðe wisman. & swiðe rice. & wurðfulre and strengere þonne ænig his foregenga wære. "[('', '1086.')]",He wæs milde þam godum mannum þe God lufedon. & ofer eall gemett stearc þam mannum þe wiðcwædon his willan. "[('', '1086.')]",On ðam ilcan steode þe God him geuðe þæt he moste Engleland gegan. he arerde mære mynster. & munecas þær gesætte. & hit wæll gegodade. "[('', '1086.')]",On his dagan wæs þæt mære mynster on Cantwarbyrig getymbrad. & eac swiðe manig oðer ofer eall Englaland. "[('', '1086.')]",Eac þis land wæs swiðe afylled mid munecan. & þa leofodan heora lif æfter sanctus Benedictus regule. "[('', '1086.')]",& se Cristendom wæs swilc on his dæge þæt ælc man hwæt his hade to belumpe. folgade se þe wolde. "[('', '1086.')]",Eac he wæs swyðe wurðful. þriwa he bær his cynehelm ælce geare. swa oft swa he wæs on Englelande. "[('', '1086.')]",On Eastron he hine bær on Winceastre. on Pentecosten on Westmynstre. on midewintre on Gleaweceastre. "[('', '1086.')]",& þænne wæron mid him ealle þa rice men ofer eall Englaland. arcebiscopas. & leodbiscopas. abbodas & eorlas. þegnas & cnihtas. "[('', '1086.')]",Swilce he wæs eac swyðe stearc man & ræðe. swa þæt man ne dorste nan þing ongean his willan don. "[('', '1086.')]",He hæfde eorlas on his bendum. þe dydan ongean his willan. "[('', '1086.')]",Biscopas he sætte of heora biscoprice. & abbodas of heora abbodrice. & þægnas on cweartern. & æt nextan he ne sparode his agenne broðor. Odo het. "[('', '1086.')]",He wæs swiðe rice biscop on Normandige. on Baius wæs his biscopstol. & wæs manna fyrmest toeacan þam cynge. "[('', '1086.')]",& he hæfde eorldom on Englelande. & þonne se cyng on Normandige. þonne wæs he mægest on þisum lande. "[('', '1086.')]",& hine he sætte on cweartern. "[('', '1086.')]",Betwyx oðrum þingum nis na to forgytane þæt gode frið þe he macode on þisan lande. swa þæt an man þe him sylf aht wære. mihte faran ofer his rice mid his bosum full goldes ungederad. & nan man ne dorste slean oðerne man. næfde he næfre swa mycel yfel gedon wið þone oðerne. "[('', '1086.')]",& Gif hwilc carl man hæmde wið Wimman hire unðances. sona he forleas þa limu þe he mid pleagode. "[('', '1086.')]",He rixade ofer Englæland. & hit mid his geapscipe swa þurhsmeade. þæt næs an hid landes innan Englælande. þæt he nyste hwa heo hæfde. oððe hwæs heo wurð wæs. & syððan on his gewrit gesætt. "[('', '1086.')]",Brytland him wæs on gewealde. & he þær inne casteles gewrohte. & þet Manncynn mid ealle gewealde. "[('', '1086.')]",Swilce eac Scotland he him underþædde. for his mycele strengþe. "[('', '1086.')]",Normandige þæt land wæs his gecynde. "[('', '1086.')]",& ofer þone eorldom þe Mans is gehaten he rixade. "[('', '1086.')]",& Gif he moste þa gyt twa gear libban. he hæfde Yrlande mid his werscipe gewunnon. & wiðutan ælcon wæpnon. "[('', '1086.')]",Witodlice on his timan hæfdon men mycel geswinc. & swiðe manige teonan. "[('', '1086.')]",Castelas he let wyrcean & earme men swiðe swencean. "[('', '1086.')]",Se cyng wæs swa swiðe stearc & benam of his underþeoddan man manig marc goldes & ma hundred punda seolfres. "[('', '1086.')]",Ðet he nam be wihte & mid mycelan unrihte of his landleode for neode. "[('', '1086.')]",He wæs on gitsunge befeallan & grædinæsse he lufode mid ealle. "[('', '1086.')]","He sætte mycel deorfrið & he lægde laga þærwið, þæt swa hwa swa sloge heort oððe hinde, þæt hine man sceolde blendian." "[('', '1086.')]","He forbead þa heortas swylce eac þa baras, swa swiðe he lufode þa headeor swilce he wære heora fæder." "[('', '1086.')]",Eac he sætte be þam haran þæt hi mosten freo faran. "[('', '1086.')]",His rice men hit mændon & þa earme men hit beceorodan. "[('', '1086.')]","Ac he swa stið þæt he ne rohte heora eallra nið, ac hi moston mid ealle þes cynges wille folgian, gif hi woldon libban oððe land habban, land oððe eahta oððe wel his sehta." "[('', '1086.')]","Wala wa, þæt ænig man sceolde modigan swa hine sylf upp ahebban & ofer ealle men tellan." "[('', '1086.')]",Se ælmihtiga God cyþæ his saule mildheortnisse & do him his synna forgifenesse. "[('', '1086.')]",Ðas þing we habbað be him gewritene. ægðer ge gode ge yfele. þæt þa godan men niman æfter þeora godnesse. & forleon mid ealle yfelnesse. & gan on ðone weg. þe us lett to heofonan rice. "[('', '1086.')]",Fela þinga we magon writan þe on ðam ilcan geare gewordene wæron. "[('', '1086.')]",Swa hit wæs on Denmearcan. þæt þa Dænescan þe wæs ærur geteald eallra folca getreowast. wurdon awende to þære meste untriwðe. & to þam mæsten swicdome þe æfre mihte gewurðan. "[('', '1086.')]",Hi gecuron & abugan to Cnute cynge. & him aðas sworon. & syððan hine earhlice ofslogon innan anre cyrcean. "[('', '1086.')]",Eac wearð on Ispanie þæt þa hæðenan men foran & hergodan uppon þam Cristenan mannan. & mycel abegdan to heora anwealde. "[('', '1086.')]","Ac se Cristena cyng, Anphos wæs gehaten, he sende ofer eall into ælcan lande. & gyrnde fultumes. & him com to fultum of ælcen lande þe Cristen wæs, & ferdon & ofslogon & aweg adrifan eall þet hæðena folc. & gewunnon heora land ongean. þurh Godes fultum." "[('', '1086.')]",Eac on þisan ilcan lande on þam ilcan geare. forðferdon manega rice men. Stigand biscop of Ciceastre. & se abbod of sancte Augustine. & se abbod of Baðon. & þe of Perscoran. & ða heora eallra hlaford Willelm Englælandes cyng. þe we ær beforan embe spæcon. "[('', '1086.')]",Æfter his deaðe his sune. Willelm hæt eallswa þe fæder. feng to þam rice & wearð gebletsod to cynge fram Landfrance arcebiscop on Westmynstre. þreom dagum ær Michaeles mæssedæg. & ealle þa men on Englalande him to abugon. & him aðas sworon. "[('', '1086.')]",Ðisum þus gedone. se cyng ferde to Winceastre. & sceawode þæt madmehus. & þa gersuman þe his fæder ær gegaderode. "[('', '1086.')]",Þa wæron unasecgendlice ænie men hu mycel þær wæs gegaderod. on golde & on seolfre. & on faton. & on pællan. & on gimman. & on manige oðre deorwurðe þingon. þe earfoðe sindon to ateallene. "[('', '1086.')]",Se cyng dyde þa swa his fæder him bebead ær he dead wære. dælde þa gersuman for his fæder saule. to ælcen mynstre þe wes innan Englelande to suman mynstrexmarc goldes. to sumanvi& to ælcen cyrcean uppe landlxpænega. & into ælcere scire man seonde hundred punda feos. to dælanne earme mannan for his saule. "[('', '1086.')]",& ær he forðferde he bead þæt man sceolde unlesan ealle þa menn þe on hæftnunge wæron under his anwealde. "[('', '1086.')]",& se cyng wæs on ðam midewintre on Lundene. "[('', '1087.')]",On þisum geare wæs þis land swiðe astirad. & mid mycele swicdome afylled. swa þæt þa riceste Frencisce men þe weron innan þisan lande. wolden swican heora hlaforde þam cynge. & woldon habban his broðer to cynge Rodbeard þe wæs eorl on Normandige. "[('', '1087.')]",On þisum ræde wæs ærest Oda biscop. & Gosfrið biscop. & Willelm biscop on Dunholme. "[('', '1087.')]",Swa wæll dyde se cyng be þam biscop. þæt eall Englaland færde æfter his ræde. & swa swa he wolde. & he þohte to donne be him eall swa Iudas Scarioth dyde be ure Drihtene. "[('', '1087.')]",& Rogere eorl wæs eac æt þam unræde. & swiðe mycel folc mid heom ealle Frencisce men. & þæs unræd wærð geræd innan þam lengtene. "[('', '1087.')]",Sona swa hit com to þam Eastron. þa ferdon hi & hergodon & bærndon & aweston þæs cynges feormehames. & eallra þæra manna land hi fordydon þe wæron innan þæs cynges holdscipe. "[('', '1087.')]",& heora ælc ferde to his castele. & þone mannoden & metsoden swa hig betst mihton. "[('', '1087.')]",Gosfrið biscop & Rodbeard a Mundbræg ferdon to Bricgstowe & hergodon & brohton to þam castele þa hergunge. & syððon foron ut of ðam castele & hergodon Baðon. & eall þæt land þær abutan. & eall Beorclea hyrnesse hi awæston. "[('', '1087.')]",& ða men þe yldest wæron of Hereforde. & eall þeo scir forð mid. & þa men of Scrobscyre mid mycele folce of Brytlande comon & hergodon & bærndon on Wiðreceastrescire forð þæt hi comon to þam porte sylfan. & woldon þa ðæne port bærnen. & þæt mynster reafian. & þæs cynges castel gewinnan heom to handa. "[('', '1087.')]",Ðas þing geseonde se arwurða biscop Wlstan. wearð swiðe gedrefed on his mode. forðig him wæs betæht þe castel to healdene. "[('', '1087.')]",Þeah hweðer his hired men ferdon ut mid feawe mannan of þam castele. & þurh Godes mildheortnisse & þurh þæs biscopas geearnunga ofslogon & gelæhton fif hundred manna. & þa oðre ealle aflymdon. "[('', '1087.')]",Se biscop of Dunholme dyde to hearme þæt he mihte ofer eall be norðan. "[('', '1087.')]",Roger het an of heom. se hleop into þam castele æt Norðwic. & dyde git eallra wærst ofer eall þæt land. "[('', '1087.')]",Hugo eac an þe hit ne gebette nan þing. ne innan Lægreceastrescire. ne innan Norðhamtune. "[('', '1087.')]",Ðe biscop Odo þe þas þyng of awocan ferde into Cent to his eorldome. & fordyde hit swyðe. & þæs cynges land. & þæs arcebiscopas mid ealle aweston. & brohte eall þæt god into his castele on Hrofeceastre. "[('', '1087.')]",Ða þe cyng undergeat ealle þas þing. & hwilcne swicdom hi dydon toweard his. þa wearð he on his mode swiðe gedrefed. "[('', '1087.')]",Sende þa æfter Englisce mannan. & heom foresæde his neode. & gyrnde heora fultumes. "[('', '1087.')]",& behet heom þa betsta laga þa æfre ær wæs on þisan lande. & ælc geold he forbead. & geatte mannan heora wudas. and slætinge. ac hit ne stod nane hwile. "[('', '1087.')]",Ac Englisce men swa þeah fengon to þam cynge heora hlaforde on fultume. "[('', '1087.')]",Ferdon þa toweard Hrofeceastre. & woldon þone biscop Odan begytan. þohtan gif hi hæfdon hine þe wæs ærur heafod to ðam unræde. þæt hi mihton þe bet begytan ealla þa oðre. "[('', '1087.')]",Hi comon þa to þam castele to Tonebricge. þa wæron innan þam castele Oda biscopes cnihtas. & oðre manige þe hine healdon woldan ongean þone cyng. "[('', '1087.')]",Ac þa Englisce men ferdon. & tobræcon þone castel. & þa men þe þærinne wæron. griðodon wið þone cyng. "[('', '1087.')]",Se cyng mid his here ferde toweard Hrofeceastre. & wendon þæt se biscop wære þærinne. ac hit wearð þam cynge cuð þet se biscop wæs afaren to ðam castele a Pefenesea. "[('', '1087.')]",& se cyng mid his here ferde æfter. & besætt þone castel abutan. mid swiðe mycele here fulle six wucan. "[('', '1087.')]",Betwyx þissum se eorl of Normandige Rodbeard þes cynges broðer gaderode swiðe mycel folc. & þohte to gewinnane Engleland mid þæra manna fultume þe wæron innan þisan lande ongean þone cyng. & he sende of his mannan to þisum lande. & wolde cuman himsylf æfter. "[('', '1087.')]",Ac þa Englisce men þe wærdedon þære sæ. gelæhton of þam mannon. & slogon. & adrengton ma þonne ænig man wiste to tellanne. "[('', '1087.')]",Syððan heom ateorede mete wiðinnan þam castele. ða hi griðas. & agefan hine þam cynge. "[('', '1087.')]",& se biscop swor þæt he wolde ut of Englelande faran. & na mare cuman on ðisan lande butan se cyng him æfter sende. & þæt he wolde agifan þone castel on Hrofeceastre. "[('', '1087.')]",Ealswa se biscop ferde & sceolde agifan þone castel. & se cyng sende his men mid him. "[('', '1087.')]",Ða arisan þa men þe wæron innan þam castele. & namon þone biscop & þes cynges men. & dydon hi on hæftnunge. "[('', '1087.')]",Innan þam castele wæron swiðe gode cnihtas. Eustatius þe iunga. & Rogeres eorles þreo sunan. & ealle þa betstboren men. þe wæron innan þisan lande. oððe on Normandige. "[('', '1087.')]","Ða se cyng undergeat þas þing. þa ferde he æfter mid þam here þe he ðær hæfde. & sende ofer eall Englalande. & bead þæt ælc man þe wære unniðing sceolde cuman to him, Frencisce & Englisce. of porte & of uppelande." "[('', '1087.')]",Him com þa mycel folc to. & he for Hrofeceastre. & besætt þone castel. oððet hi griðedon þæ þær inne wæron. & þone castel ageafon. "[('', '1087.')]",Se biscop Odo mid þam mannum þe innan þam castele wæron ofer sæ ferdon. & se biscop swa forlet þone wurðscipe þe he on þis land hæfde. "[('', '1087.')]",Se cyng syððan sende here to Dunholme. & let besittan þone castel. & se biscop griðode and ageaf þone castel. & forlet his biscoprice. & ferde to Normandige. "[('', '1087.')]",Eac manige Frencisce men forleton heora land. & ferdon ofer sæ. & se cyng geaf heora land þam mannum þe him holde wæron. "[('', '1089.')]",On þisum geare se arwurða muneca feder & frouer Landfranc arcebiscop gewat of þissum life. ac we hopiað þæt he ferde to þæt heofanlice rice. "[('', '1089.')]",Swilce eac gewarð ofer eall Engleland mycel eorðstyrunge. on þone dægiii IDus Augustus. "[('', '1089.')]",& wæs swiðe lætsum gear on corne. & on ælces cynnes wæstmum. swa þæt manig men ræpon heora corn onbutan Martines mæssan. & gyt lator. "[('', '1090.')]",INDICTIONE XIII. "[('', '1090.')]",Ðissum þus gedon. eall swa wæ ær abufan sædan be þam cynge. & be his broðer. & be his mannon. Se cyng wæs smægende hu he mihte wrecon his broðer Rodbeard swiðost swencean. & Normandige of him gewinnan. "[('', '1090.')]",Ðeah þurh his geapscipe. oððe þurh gærsuma he begeat þone castel æt sancte Waleri. & þa hæfenan. "[('', '1090.')]",& swa he begeat þone æt Albemare. & þarinne he sette his cnihtas. & hi dydon hearmes uppon þam lande on hergunge & on bærnete. "[('', '1090.')]",Æfter þisum he begeat ma castelas innan þam lande. & þær inne his rideras gelogode. "[('', '1090.')]",Se eorl of Normandige Rodbeard syððan he undergeat þæt his gesworene men him trucedon. & agefon hera castelas him to hearme. þa sende he to his hlaforde Philippe Francena cynge. & he com to Normandige mid mycelan here. "[('', '1090.')]",& se cyng & se eorl mid ormætre fyrde besæton þone castel abuton. þær þæs cynges men of Engleland inne wæron. "[('', '1090.')]",Se cyng Willelm of Englalande sende to Philippe Francena cynge. & he for his lufan oððe for his mycele gersuma forlet swa his man þone eorl Rodbeard & his land. & ferde ongean to France & let heom swa weorðan. "[('', '1090.')]",& betwyx þisum þingum þis land wæs swiðe fordon. on unlagagelde. & on oðre manige ungelimpe. "[('', '1091.')]",On þisum geare se cyng Willelm heold his hired to Cristes messan on Wæstmynstre. & þær æfter to Candelmæssan he ferde for his broðær unþearfe ut of Englalande into Normandige. "[('', '1091.')]",Onmang þam þe he þær wæs. heora sehte togædere eode. on þæt gerad þæt se eorl him to handan let Uescam. & þone eorldom æt Ou. & Kiæresburh. And þærtoeacan þes cynges men sacleas beon moston. on þam castelan. þe hi ær þes eorles unþances begiten hæfdon. "[('', '1091.')]","& Se cyng him ongean þa Manige behet, þe ær heora fæder gewann. & þa fram þam eorle gebogen wæs, gebygle to donne. & eall þæt his fæder þær begeondan hæfde. butan þam þe he <þam> cynge þa geunnen hæfde." "[('', '1091.')]",& þæt ealle þa þe on Englelande for þam eorle æror heora land forluron. hit on þisum sehte habban sceoldan. & se eorl on Englelande eall swa mycel swa on heora forewarde wæs. "[('', '1091.')]",And gif se eorl forðferde butan sunu be rihtre æwe. wære se cyng yrfenuma of eallon Normandig. Be þisre sylfan forewarde gif se cyng swulte. wære se eorl yrfenuma ealles Englalandes. "[('', '1091.')]",Ðas forewarde gesworanxiiþa betste of þes cynges healfe. andxiiof þes eorles. þeah hit syððan litle hwile stode. "[('', '1091.')]",On mang þisum sæhte wearð Eadgar æþeling belandod. of þam þe se eorl him æror þær to handa gelæten hæfde. & ut of Normandig for to þam cynge his aðume to Scotlande. & to his swustor. "[('', '1091.')]",On mang þam þe se cyng Willelm ut of Englelande wæs. ferde se cyng Melcolm of Scotlande hider into Englum. & his mycelne dæl oferhergode. oð þæt þa gode mæn þe þis land bewiston. him fyrde ongean sændon. & hine gecyrdon. "[('', '1091.')]",Ða þa se cyng Willelm into Normandige þis gehyrde. þa gearcode he his fare. & to Englelande com. & his broðer se eorl Rodbeard mid him. "[('', '1091.')]",& sona fyrde het ut abeodan. ægðer scipfyrde & landfyrde. ac seo scipfyrde ær he to Scotlande cuman mihte. ælmæst earmlice forfor. feowan dagon toforan sancte Michæles mæssan. "[('', '1091.')]",And se cyng & his broðer mid þære landfyrde ferdon. ac þa ða se cyng Melcolm gehyrde þæt hine man mid fyrde secean wolde. he for mid his fyrde ut of Scotlande into Loðene on Englaland & þær abad. "[('', '1091.')]",Ða þa se cyng Willelm mid his fyrde genealehte. þa ferdon betwux Rodbeard eorl & Eadgar æðeling & þæra cinga sehte swa gemacedon. þæt se cyng Melcolm to uran cynge com. & his man wearð to eallswilcre gehyrsumnisse swa he ær his fæder dyde. & þæt mid aðe gefestnode. "[('', '1091.')]",& se cyng Willelm him behet on lande & on ealle þinge þæs þe he under his fæder ær hæfde. "[('', '1091.')]",On þisum sehte wearð eac Eadgar eþeling wið þone cyng gesæhtlad. & þa cyngas þa mid mycclum sehte tohwurfon. ac þæt litle hwile stod. "[('', '1091.')]",And se eorl Rodbeard her oð Cristes mæsse forneah mid þam cynge wunode. & litel soðes þær on mang. of heora forewarde onfand. & twam dagon ær þære tide on Wiht scipode. & into Normandig for. & Eadgar æðeling mid him. "[('', '1092.')]",On þisum geare se cyng Willelm mid mycelre fyrde ferde norð to Cardeol. & þa burh geæðstaþelede. & þone castel arerde. & Dolfin utadraf þe æror þær þes landes weold. & þone castel mid his mannan gesette. "[('', '1092.')]",& syððan hider suð gewænde. & mycele mænige Eyrlisces folces mid wifa & mid orfe þyder sænde. þær to wunigenne þæt land to tilianne. "[('', '1093.')]",On þisum geare to þam længtene warð se cyng Willelm on Gleaweceastre to þam swiðe geseclod. þæt he wæs ofer eall dead gekyd. "[('', '1093.')]",& on his broke he Gode fela behæsa behet. his agen lif on riht to lædene. & Godes cyrcean griðian & friðian. & næfre ma eft wið feo gesyllan. & ealle rihte lage on his þeode to habbene. "[('', '1093.')]",And þæt on Cantwarbyrig þe ær on his agenre hand stod. Anselme betæhte. se wæs ær on Bæc. & Rodbeard his cancelere þæt biscoprice on Lincolne. "[('', '1093.')]",& to manegan mynstren land geuðe. ac þæt he syððan ætbræd. þa him gebotad wæs. & ealle þa gode laga forlæt. þe he us ær behet. "[('', '1093.')]",Ða æfter þisson sende cyng of Scotlande. & þære forewarde gyrnde þe him behaten wæs. "[('', '1093.')]",And se cing Willelm him steofnode to Gloweceastre. & him to Scotlande gislas sende. & Eadgar æþeling æfter. & þa men syððan ongean. þe hine mid mycclon wurðscipe to þam cynge brohtan. "[('', '1093.')]",Ac þa ða he to þam cynge com ne mihte he beon weorðe naðer ne ure cynges spæce. ne þæra forewarde þe him ær behatene wæron. & forþi hi þa mid mycelon unsehte tohwurfon. & se cyng Melcolm ham to Scotlande gewænde. "[('', '1093.')]",Ac hraðe þæs þe he ham com. he his fyrde gegaderode. & into Englelande hergende mid maran unræde ferde þone him abehofode. & hine þa Rodbeard se eorl of Norðhymbran mid his mannan unwæres besyrede & ofsloh. "[('', '1093.')]",Hine sloh Moræl of Bæbbaburh. se wæs þæs eorles stiward. & Melcolmes cynges godsib. "[('', '1093.')]",Mid him wæs eac Eadward his sune ofslagen. se æfter him cyng beon sceolde. gif he hit gelifode. "[('', '1093.')]",Ða þa seo gode cwen Margarita þis gehyrde. hyre þa leofstan hlaford & sunu þus beswikene. heo wearð oð deað on mode geancsumed. & mid hire prestan to cyrcean eode. & hire gerihtan underfeng. & æt Gode abæd. þæt heo hire gast ageaf. "[('', '1093.')]",& ða Scottas þa Dufenal to cynge gecuron Melcolmes broðer. & ealle þa Englisce ut adræfdon. þe ær mid þam cynge Melcolme wæron. "[('', '1093.')]",Ða þa Dunecan Melcolmes cynges sunu þis eall gehyrde þus gefaren. se on þæs cynges hyrede Willelmes wæs. swa swa his fæder hine ures cynges fæder ær to gisle geseald hæfde. & her swa syððan belaf. he to þam cynge com. "[('', '1093.')]",& swilce getrywða dyde. swa se cyng æt him habban wolde. & swa mid his unne to Scotlande for. mid þam fultume þe he begytan mihte Engliscra & Frenciscra. and his mæge Dufenal þes rices benam. & to cynge wearð underfangen. "[('', '1093.')]",Ac þa Scottas hi eft sume gegaderoden. & forneah ealle his mænu ofslogan. & he sylf mid feawum ætbærst. "[('', '1093.')]",Syððan hi wurdon sehte. on þa gerad þæt he næfre eft Englisce ne Frencisce into þam lande ne gelogige. "[('', '1094.')]",Her hæfde se cyng Willelm to Cristes mæssan his hired æt Gleaweceastre. & him þider fram his broðer Rodbearde of Normandig bodan coman. "[('', '1094.')]",Þa cyddon þæt his broðer grið & forewarde eall æfter cwæð. butan se cyng gelæstan wolde eall þet hi on forewarde hæfdon ær gewroht. & uppon þæt hine forsworenne & trywleasne clypode. buton he þa forewarda geheolde. oððe þider ferde & hine þær betealde þær seo forewarde ær wæs gewroht & eac gesworen. "[('', '1094.')]",Ða ferde se cyng to Hæstingan to þam Candelmæssan. & on mang þam þe he þær wederes abad. he let halgian þæt mynster æt þære Bataille. & Herbearde Losange þam biscop of þeotfordan his stæf benam. "[('', '1094.')]",& þær æfter to midlengtene ofer sæ for into Normandige. "[('', '1094.')]",Syððan he þider com. he & his broðer Rodbeard se eorl gecwæðan. þæt hi mid griðe togædere cuman sceoldan. & swa dydon. & gesemede beon ne mihtan. "[('', '1094.')]",Syððan eft hi togædere coman mid þam ilcan mannan þe ær þæt loc makedon. & eac þa aðas sworen. & ealne þone bryce uppon þone cyng tealdon. ac he nolde þæs geþafa beon. ne eac þa forewarde healdan. & forþam hi þa mid mycelon unsehte tocyrdon. "[('', '1094.')]",And se cyng syððan þone castel æt Bures gewann. & þes eorles men þær inne genam. þa sume to lande sende. "[('', '1094.')]",Ðær togeanes se eorl mid þes cynges fultume of France gewann þone castel æt Argentses. & þearinne Rogger Peiteuin genam. & seofen hundred þes cynges cnihta mid him. & syððan þone æt Hulme. "[('', '1094.')]",& Oft rædlice heora ægðer uppon oðerne tunas bærnde. & eac menne læhte. "[('', '1094.')]",Ða sende cyng hider to lande. & het abeodan utxxþusenda Engliscra manna him to fultume to Normandig. ac þa hi to sæ coman. þa het hi man cyrran. & þæt feoh syllan to þæs cynges behofe þe hi genumen hæfdon. þet wæs ælc man healf punda. & hi swa dydon. "[('', '1094.')]",& se eorl innon Normandig æfter þison mid þam cynge of France. & mid eallon þan þe hi gegaderian mihton ferdon towardes Ou þær se cyng Willelm inne wæs. & þohtan hine inne to besittanne. & swa foran oð hi coman to Lungeuile. "[('', '1094.')]",Ðær wearð se cyng of France þurh gesmeah gecyrred. & swa syððan eall seo fyrding tohwearf. "[('', '1094.')]",Her onmang þison se cyng Willelm sende æfter his broðer Heanrige. se wæs on þam castele æt Damfront. ac forþi þe he mid friðe þurh Normandig faran ne mihte. he him sende scipon æfter. & Hugo eorl of Ceastre. "[('', '1094.')]",Ac þa ða hi towardes Ou faran sceoldan þær se cyng wæs. hi foran to Englelande. & up coman æt Hamtune on ealra halgena mæsseæfne. & her syððon wunedon. & to Cristes mæssan wæron on Lunden. "[('', '1094.')]",Eac on þisum ylcan geare þa Wylisce menn hi gegaderodon. & wið þa Frencisce þe on Walon. oððe on þære neawiste wæron & hi ær belandedon. gewinn upahofon. & manige festena & castelas abræcon. & men ofslogon. "[('', '1094.')]",An syððan heora gefylce weox. hi hi on ma todældon. "[('', '1094.')]",Wið sum þæra dæle gefeaht Hugo eorl of Scrobscire & hi aflymde. "[('', '1094.')]",Ac þeah hweðer þa oðre. ealles þæs geares nanes yfeles ne geswicon þe hi don mihton. "[('', '1094.')]",Ðises geares eac þa Scottas heora cyng Dunecan besyredon & ofslogan. & heom syððan eft oðre syðe his fæderan Dufenal to cynge genamon. þurh þes lare & to tihtinge he wearð to deaðe beswicen. "[('', '1095.')]",On þisum geare wæs se cyng Willelm to Cristes mæssan þa feower forewarde dagas on Hwitsand. & æfter þam feorðan dæge hider to lande for. & upp com æt Doferan. "[('', '1095.')]",And Heanrig þes cynges broðer her on lande oð lengten wunode. & þa ofer sæ for to Normandig mid mycclon gersuman. on þæs cynges heldan uppon heora broðer Rodbeard eorl. "[('', '1095.')]",& gelomlice uppon þone eorl wann. & him mycelne hearm ægðer on lande & on mannan dyde. "[('', '1095.')]",And þa to Eastran heold se cyng his hired on Winceastre. & se eorl Rodbeard of Norðhymbran nolde to hirede cuman. "[('', '1095.')]",& se cyng forðan wearð wið hine swiðe astyrod. & him to sænde & heardlice bead gif he griðes weorðe beon wolde. þæt he to Pentecosten to hired come. "[('', '1095.')]",On þisum geare wæron Eastron onviii kalendæ Aprilis. "[('', '1095.')]",& þa uppon Eastron on sancte Ambrosius mæsse niht. þæt isii Nonæ Apriliswæs gesewen forneah ofer eall þis land swilce forneah ealle þa niht swiðe mænifealdlice steorran of heofenan feollan. naht be anan oððe twam. ac swa þiclice þæt hit nan mann ateallan ne mihte. "[('', '1095.')]",Her æfter to Pentecosten wæs se cyng on Windlesoran. & ealle his witan mid him. butan þam eorle of Norðhymbran. forþam se cyng him naþer nolde ne gislas syllan. ne uppon trywðan geunnon þæt he mid griðe cumon moste & faran. "[('', '1095.')]",& se cyng forþi his fyrde bead. & uppon þone eorl to Norðhymbran for. "[('', '1095.')]",& sona þes þe he þider com. he manege & forneah ealle þa betste of þes eorles hirede innan anan fæstene gewann. & on hæftene gedyde. "[('', '1095.')]",& þone castel æt Tinemuðan besæt oððet he hine gewann. & þæs eorles broðer þærinne & ealle þa þe him mid wæron. and syððan ferde to Bebbaburh. & þone eorl þærinne besæt. "[('', '1095.')]",Ac þa ða se cyng geseah þæt he hine gewinnan ne mihte. þa het he makian ænne castel toforan Bebbaburh. & hine on his spæce Malueisin het. þæt is on Englisc Yfel nehhebur. "[('', '1095.')]",& hine swiðe mid his mannan gesætte. & syððan suðweard for. "[('', '1095.')]",Ða sona æfter þam þe se cyng wæs suð afaren. feorde se eorl anre nihte ut of Bebbaburh towardes Tinemuðan. "[('', '1095.')]",Ac þa þe innan þam niwan castele wæron. his gewær wurdon. & him æfter foran & onfuhton. & hine gewundedon. & syððan gelæhton. & þa þe mid him wæron sume ofslogan. sume lifes gefengon. "[('', '1095.')]", þison wearð þam cynge cuð. þæt þa Wylisce men on Wealon sumne castel heafdon tobroken Muntgumni hatte. & Hugon eorles menn ofslagene þe hine healdon sceoldan. "[('', '1095.')]",& he forþi oðre fyrde het fearlice abannan. & æfter sancte Michaelesmæsse into Wealan ferde. "[('', '1095.')]",& his fyrde toscyfte. & þæt land eall þurhfor. swa þæt seo fyrde eall togædere com to ealra halgena to Snawdune. "[('', '1095.')]",Ac þa Wylisce a toforan into muntan and moran ferdan þæt heom man to cuman ne mihte. & se cyng þa hamweard gewende forþam he geseah þæt he þær þes wintres mare don ne mihte. "[('', '1095.')]",Ða þa se cyng ongean com. þa het he niman þone eorl Rotbeard of Norðhymbran & to Bæbbaburh lædan. & ægðer eage utadon. buton þa þe þær inne wæron þone castel agyfan woldan. "[('', '1095.')]",Hine heoldan his wif. & Moreal se wæs stiward & eac his mæg. "[('', '1095.')]",Ðurh þis wearð se castel þa agyfen. & Moreal wearð þa on þes cynges hirede. & þurh hine wurdon manege ægðer ge gehadode & eac læwede geypte. þe mid heora ræde on þes cynges unheldan wæron. "[('', '1095.')]",Þa se cyng sume ær þære tide het on hæftneðe gebringan. & syððan swiðe gemahlice ofer eall þis land beodan. þæt ealle þa þe of þam cynge land heoldan. eall swa hi friðes weorðe beon woldan. þæt hi on hirede to tide wæron. "[('', '1095.')]",And þone eorl Rotbert het se cyng to Windlesoran lædan. & þær innan þam castele healdan. "[('', '1095.')]",Eac on þis ylcan geare togeanes Eastron com þæs Papan sande hider to lande. þæt wæs Waltear bisceop swiðe god lifes man of Albin þære ceastre. & þam Ansealme uppon Pentecosten of þæs Papan healfe Urbanus his pallium geaf. "[('', '1095.')]",& he hine underfeng æt his arcestole on Cantwarabyrig. and se biscop Waltear her on lande þæs geares syððan lange wunode. & man syððan þæt Rom gesceot be him sende. swa man manegan gearan æror ne dyde. "[('', '1095.')]",Ðises ylcan eac geares wæron swiðe untid gewidera. & forþi geond eall þis land wurdon eorðwæstmas eall to medemlice gewende. "[('', '1096.')]",On þison geare heold se cyng Willelm his hired to Cristes mæssan on Windlesoran. "[('', '1096.')]",& Willelm biscop of Dunholme þær forðferde to geares dæge. "[('', '1096.')]",And on Octabris Epiphanis wæs se cyng & ealle his witan on Searbyrig. "[('', '1096.')]",Þær beteah Gosfrei Bainard Willelm of Ou þes cynges mæg þæt he heafde gebeon on þes cynges swicdome. & hit him on gefeaht. & hine on orreste ofercom. "[('', '1096.')]",& syððan he ofercumen wæs. him het se cyng þa eagan utadon. & syþðan belisnian. "[('', '1096.')]",& his stiward Willelm hatte. se wæs his modrian sunu. het se cyng on rode ahon. "[('', '1096.')]",Ðær wearð eac Eoda eorl of Campaine þæs cynges aðum & manege oðre belende. & sumne man to Lundene lædde. & þær spilde. "[('', '1096.')]",Ðises geares eac to þam Eastran wearð swiðe mycel styrung geond ealle þas þeode. & fela oðra þeodan þurh Urbanus se wæs Papa gehaten þeah þe he þæs setles naþing næfde on Rome. "[('', '1096.')]",& ferde unarimedlice folc mid wifan & cildan to þi þæt hi uppon hæðene þeodan winnan woldan. "[('', '1096.')]",Ðurh þas fare wearð se cyng & his broðor Rodbeard eorl sehte. swa þæt se cyng ofer sæ for. & eall Normandig æt him mid feo alisde. swa swa hi þa sehte wæron. "[('', '1096.')]",And se eorl syððan ferde. & mid him se eorl of Flandran. & se of Bunan. & eac manige oðre heafodmen. & se eorl Rotbeard & þa þe mid him ferdon þone winter on Puille wunedon. "[('', '1096.')]",Ac þes folces þe be Hungrie for. fela þusenda þær & be wæge earmlice forforan. & fela hreowlice & hungerbitene ongean winterham tugon. "[('', '1096.')]",Ðis wæs swiðe hefigtime gear geond eall Angelcyn. ægðer ge þurh mænigfealde gylda. & eac þurh swiðe hefigtymne hunger. þe þisne eard þæs geares swiðe gedrehte. "[('', '1096.')]",Eac on þison geare þa heafodmen þe þis land heoldan oft rædlice fyrde into Wealon sendon. & mænig man mid þam swiðe gedrehtan. ac man þær ne gespædde. butan manmyrringe. & feohspillinge. "[('', '1097.')]",Her on þison geare weas se cyng Willelm to Cristes mæssan on Normandig. & þa togeanes Eastron hider to lande for. forþam he þohte his hired on Winceastre to healdenne. "[('', '1097.')]",Ac he wearð þurh weder gelet. oððet Eastre æfen þæt he up com ærost æt Arundel. & forþi his hired æt Windlesoran heold. "[('', '1097.')]",& þær æfter mid mycclum here into Wealon ferde. & þæt land swiðe mid his fyrde þurhfor. þurh sume þa Wyliscean þe him to wæron cumen & his lædteowas wæron. "[('', '1097.')]",& þærinne wunode fram middesumeran forneah oð August. & mycel þærinne forleas on mannan & on horsan. & eac on manegan oðran þingan. "[('', '1097.')]",Ða Wylisce men syððon hi fram þam cynge gebugon. heom manege ealdras of heom sylfan gecuron. sum þæra wæs Caduugaun gehaten þe heora weorðast wæs. se wæs Griffines broðer sunu cynges. "[('', '1097.')]",Ac þa ða se cyng geseah þæt he nan þingc his willes þær geforðian ne mihte. he ongean into þison lande for. & hraðe æfter þam. he be þam gemæron castelas let gemakian. "[('', '1097.')]",Ða uppon sancte Michaeles mæssaniiii Nonæ Octobrisætywde an selcuð steorra on æfen scynende & sona to setle gangende. "[('', '1097.')]",He wæs gesewen suðweast. & se leoma þe him ofstod. wæs swiðe lang geþuht suðeast scinende. & forneah ealle þa wucan on þas wisan ætywde. "[('', '1097.')]",Manige men leton þæt hit cometa wære. "[('', '1097.')]",Sona æfter þyson. se arcebiscop Ansealm of Cantwarbyrig. leafe æt þam cynge nam. þeah hit þam cynge unge will wære þæs þe men leton. & ofer sæ for. forþam him þuhte þæt man on þisne þeodan lytel æfter rihte & æfter his dyhte dyde. "[('', '1097.')]",And se cyng þær æfter uppon sancte Martines mæssan ofer sæ into Normandig for. ac þa hwile þe he wederes abad. his hired innon þam sciran þær hi lagon. þone mæston hearm dydon þe æfre hired oððe here innon friðlande don sceolde. "[('', '1097.')]",Ðis wæs on eallon þingan swiðe hefigtyme gear. & ofer geswincfull. on ungewederan þa man oððe tilian sceolde. oððe eft tilða gegaderian. & on ungyldan þa næfre ne ablunnon. "[('', '1097.')]",Eac manege sciran þe mid weorce to Lundenne belumpon. wurdon þærle gedrehte. þurh þone weall þe hi worhton onbutan þone tur. & þurh þa brycge þe forneah eall toflotan wæs. & þurh þæs cynges healle geweorc þe man on Westmynstre worhte. & mænige man þær mid gedrehte. "[('', '1097.')]",Eac on þysum ylcan geare sona uppon sancte Michaeles mæssan ferde Eadgar æþeling mid fyrde þurh þæs cynges fultum into Scotlande. & þet land mid stranglicum feohte gewann. "[('', '1097.')]",& þone cyng Dufenal ut adræfde. & his mæg Eadgar se wæs Melcolmes sunu cynges & Margarite þære cwenan he þær on þæs cynges Willelmes heldan to cynge gesette. & syððan ongean into Engleland for. "[('', '1098.')]",On þysum geare to Cristes mæssan wæs se cyng Willelm on Normandig. "[('', '1098.')]",& Walcelin biscop on Winceastre. & Baldewine abbod on sancte Ædmund innan þære tide bægen forðferdan. "[('', '1098.')]",& On þisum geare eac Turold abbod of Burh forðferde. "[('', '1098.')]",Ðises geares eac to þan sumeran innan Barrucscire æt Finchamstæde an mere blod weoll. swa swa manige trywe men sædan þe hit geseon sceoldan. "[('', '1098.')]",& Hugo eorl wearð ofslagen innan Anglesege fram utwikingan. & his broðer Rodbert wearð his yrfenuma. swa swa he hit æt þam cynge ofeode. "[('', '1098.')]",Toforan sancte Michaeles mæssan ætywde seo heofon swilce heo forneah ealle þa niht byrnende wære. "[('', '1098.')]",Ðis wæs swiðe geswincfull gear þurh manigfealde ungyld. & þurh mycele renas þe ealles geares ne ablunnon. forneah ælc tilð on mersclande forferde. "[('', '1099.')]",Her wæs se cyng Willelm to midewintra on Normandig. & to Eastron hider to lande com. & to Pentecosten forman siðe his hired innan his niwan gebyttlan æt Westmynstre heold. "[('', '1099.')]",& þær Rannulfe his capellane þæt biscoprice on Dunholme geaf. þe æror ealle his gemot ofer eall Engleland draf. & bewiste. "[('', '1099.')]",& sona þær æfter ofer sæ for. & þone eorl Elias of þære Manige adraf. & hy syððan on his geweald gesætte. & swa to sancte Michaeles mæssan eft hider to lande com. "[('', '1099.')]",Ðises geares eac on sancte Martines mæssedæg. asprang up to þan swiðe sæflod. & swa mycel to hearme gedyde. swa nan man ne gemunet þæt hi æfre æror dyde. "[('', '1099.')]",& wæs ðæs ylcan dæges luna prima. "[('', '1099.')]",And Osmund biscop of Searbyrig innon Aduent forðferde. "[('', '1100.')]",On þison geare se cyng Willelm heold his hired to Cristes mæssa on Gleaweceastre. & to Eastron on Winceastre. & to Pentecosten on Westmynstre. "[('', '1100.')]",& to þam Pentecosten wæs gesewen innan Barrucscire æt anan tune blod weallan of eorþan. swa swa mænige sædan þe hit geseon sceoldan. "[('', '1100.')]",And þær æfter on morgen æfter hlammæssedæge wearð se cyng Willelm on huntnoðe fram his anan men mid anre fla ofsceoten. & syððan to Winceastre gebroht. & on þam biscoprice bebyrged. þæt wæs þæs þreotteðan geares þe he rice onfeng. "[('', '1100.')]",He wæs swiðe strang & reðe ofer his land & his mænn. & wið ealle his neahheburas. & swiðe ondrædendlic. "[('', '1100.')]",& þurh yfelra manna rædas þe him æfre gecweme wæran. & þurh his agene gitsunga. he æfre þas leode mid here & mid ungylde tyrwigende wæs. "[('', '1100.')]",Forþan þe on his dagan ælc riht afeoll. & ælc unriht for Gode & for worulde up aras. "[('', '1100.')]",Godes cyrcean he nyðerade. & þa biscoprices & abbotrices þe þa ealdras on his dagan feollan. "[('', '1100.')]",Ealle he hi oððe wið feo gesealde. oððe on his agenre hand heold. & to gafle gesette. forþan þe he ælces mannes gehadodes & læwedes yrfenuma beon wolde. "[('', '1100.')]",& swa þæt þæs dæges þe he gefeoll. he heafde on his agenre hand þæt arcebiscoprice on Cantwarbyrig. & þæt bisceoprice on Winceastre. & þæt on Searbyrig. & xi abbodrices. ealle to gafle gesette. "[('', '1100.')]",And þeah þe ic hit læng ylde. eall þet þe Gode wæs lað & rihtfullan mannan. eall þæt wæs gewunelic on þisan lande on his tyman. & forþi he wæs forneah ealre his leode lað. & Gode andsæte. "[('', '1100.')]",Swa swa his ænde ætywde. forþan þe he on middewardan his unrihte buten behreowsunge & ælcere dædbote gewat. "[('', '1100.')]",On þæne þunresdæg he wæs ofslagen. & þæs on morgen bebyrged. "[('', '1100.')]",& syðþan he bebyrged wæs. þa witan þe þa neh handa wæron. his broðer Heanrig to cynge gecuran. "[('', '1100.')]",& he þærrihte þæt biscoprice on Winceastre Willelme Giffarde geaf. & siþþan to Lundene for. "[('', '1100.')]",& on þan Sunnandæge þær æfter toforan þam weofode on Westmynstre Gode & eallan folce behet ealle þa unriht to aleggenne þe on his broðer timan wæran. & þa betstan lage to healdene þe on æniges cynges dæge toforan him stodan. "[('', '1100.')]",And hine syððan æfter þam se biscop of Lundene Mauricius to cynge gehalgode. & him ealle on þeosan lande to abugan. & aðas sworan. & his men wurdon. "[('', '1100.')]",And se cyng sona æfter þam be þære ræde þe him abutan wæran. þone biscop Rannulf of Dunholme let niman. & into þam ture on Lundene let gebringon. & þær healdan. "[('', '1100.')]",Ða toforan Sancte Michaeles mæssan com se arcebiscop Ansealm of Cantwarbyrig hider to lande. swa swa se cyng Heanrig be his witena ræde him æfter sende. forþan þe he wæs ut of þis lande gefaren. for þan mycelan unrihte þe se cyng Willelm him dyde. "[('', '1100.')]",And siðþan sona heræfter se cyng genam Mahalde him to wife Malcolmes cynges dohter of Scotlande. & Margareta þære goda cwæne Eadwardes cynges magan. & of þan rihtan Ængla landes kynekynne. "[('', '1100.')]",& on sancte Martines mæssedæg heo wearð him mid mycelan weorðscipe forgifen on Westmynstre. & se arcebiscop Ansealm hi him bewæddade. & siððan to cwene gehalgode. "[('', '1100.')]",And se arcebiscop Thomas of Eoferwic her æfter sona forðferde. "[('', '1100.')]",Ðeoses ylces geares eac innan hærfest com se eorl Rotbert ham into Normandi. & se eorl Rotbert of Flandran. & Eustatius eorl of Bunan fram Ierusalem. "[('', '1100.')]",& sona swa se eorl Rotbert into Normandig com. he wearð fram eallan þam folce bliþelice underfangen. butan þam castelan ðe wæron gesætte mid þæs cynges Heanriges manna. togeanes þan he manega gewealc & gewinn hæfde. "[('', '1101.')]",Her on þisum geare to Cristes mæssan heold se cyng Heanrig his hired on Westmynstre. & to Eastran on Winceastre. "[('', '1101.')]",& þa sona þæræfter wurdon þa heafodmen her on lande wiðerræden togeanes þam cynge. ægðer ge for heoran agenan mycelan ungetrywðan. & eac þurh þone eorl Rodbert of Normandig. þe mid unfriðe hider to lande fundode. "[('', '1101.')]",And se cyng syððan scipa ut on sæ sende his broðer to dære & to lættinge. ac hi sume æft æt þære neode abruðon. & fram þam cynge gecyrdon. & to þam eorle Rotberte gebugan. "[('', '1101.')]",Ða to midde sumeran ferde se cyng ut to Pefenesæ mid eall his fyrde togeanes his broðer & his þær abad. ac onmanig þison com se eorl Rotbert up æt Portesmuðanxiinihtan toforan Hlafmæssan. "[('', '1101.')]",& se cyng mid ealre his fyrde him togeanes com. ac þa heafod men heom betwenan foran. "[('', '1101.')]",& þa broðra gesehtodan on þa gerad. þet se cyng forlet eall þæt he mid streangðe innan Normandig togeanes þam eorle heold. & þæt ealle þa on Englelande heora land ongean heafdon. þe hit ær þurh þone eorl forluron. & Eustaties eorl eac eall his fæder land her on lande. "[('', '1101.')]",& þet se eorl Rotbert ælce geare sceolde of Englalande þreo þusend marc seolfres habban. & loc hweðer þæra gebroðra oðerne oferbide. wære yrfeweard ealles Englalandes & eac Normandiges. buton se forðfarena yrfenuman heafde be rihtre æwe. "[('', '1101.')]",& þis þa mid aðe gefestnodanxiiþa hihste of ægðre healfe. "[('', '1101.')]",And se eorl syððan oð ðet ofer sancte Michaeles mæsse her on lande wunode. & his men mycel to hearme æfre gedydon swa hi geferdon. þa hwile þe se eorl her on lande wunode. "[('', '1101.')]",Ðises geares eac se biscop Rannulf to þam Candelmæssan ut of þam ture on Lunden nihtes oðbærst þær he on hæftneðe wæs. & to Normandige for. þurh þes macunge mæst & to spryttinge se eorl Rotbert þises geares þis land mid unfriðe gesohte. "[('', '1102.')]",On þisum geare to Natiuiteð wæs se cyng Heanrig on Westmynstre. & to Eastron on Winceastre. "[('', '1102.')]",& sona þær æfter wurdon unsehte se cyng & se eorl Rotbert of Bælæsme se hæfde þone eorldom her on lande on Scrobbesbyrig þe his fæder Roger eorl ær ahte. & micel rice þærto. ægðer ge beheonon sæ ge begeondon. "[('', '1102.')]",& se cyng ferde & besæt þone castel æt Arundel. ac þa he hine swa hraðe gewinnan ne mihte. he let þær toforan castelas gemakian. & hi mid his mannan gesette. "[('', '1102.')]",& syððan mid ealre his fyrde ferde to Brigge. & þær wunode oððet he þone castel hæfde. & þone eorl Rotbert belænde. & ealles benæmde. þes he on Englalande hæfde. "[('', '1102.')]",& se eorl swa ofer sæ gewat. & se fyrde syððan ham cyrde. "[('', '1102.')]",Ða þær æfter to sancte Michaeles mæssan wæs se cyng æt Wæstmynstre. & ealle þa hæfodmen on þis lande gehadode & læwede. "[('', '1102.')]",& se arcebiscop Ansealm heold gehadodra manna sinoð. & hi þær manega beboda setton þe to Cristendome belimpað. "[('', '1102.')]",& ægðer manige Frencisce & Englisce þær heora stafas & rice forluron. þe hi mid unrihte begeaton. oððe mid woge þær on lifedon. "[('', '1102.')]",& On ðisum ylcan geare on Pentecosten mæssan wuce. þa coman þeofas sum of Aluearnie. sum of France. & sum of Flandres. & breokan þa mynstre of Burh & þærinne naman mycel to gode on golde & on seolfre. þet wæron roden & calicen & candelsticcan. "[('', '1103.')]",Her on þisum geare to midewintra wæs se cyng Heanrig æt Westmynstre. "[('', '1103.')]",& þær æfter sona ferde se biscop Willelm Giffard ut of þis land. forþan þe he ongean riht nolde his hades onfon æt þam arcebiscop Girarde of Eoferwic. "[('', '1103.')]",& þa to þan Eastran heold se cyng his hired on Winceastre. "[('', '1103.')]",& þær æfter ferde se arcebiscop Ansealm of Cantwarbyrig to Rome. swa swa him & þam cynge gewearð. "[('', '1103.')]",Ðises geares eac com se eorl Rotbert of Normandig to sprecene wið þone cyng her on lande. "[('', '1103.')]",& ær he heonne ferde he forgeaf þa þreo þusend marc þe him seo cyng Heanrig be foreweard ælce geare gifan sceolde. "[('', '1103.')]",On þisum geare eac æt Heamstede innan Barrucscire. wæs gesewen blod of eorðan. "[('', '1103.')]",Ðis wæs swiðe gedeorfsum gear her on lande. þurh mænifealde gyld.& þurh orfcwealm. & wæstma forweorþenesse ægðer ge on corne. & eac on eallon treowwæstman. "[('', '1103.')]",Eac on morgen uppon sancte Laurenties mæssedæg gedyde se wind swa mycel to hearme her on lande on eallon wæstman. swa nan man ne gemunde þæt æfre ænig ær gedyde. "[('', '1103.')]",On ðisum ylcan geare Mathias abbod of Burh forðferde. se ne lyfode na leng þan an geare. syððan he abbod wæs. "[('', '1103.')]",Æfter sancte Michaeles mæssan onxii kalendæ Novembrishe wæs mid procession underfangan to abbod. & on ðam ylcan dæge þes oðres geares he wearð dead on Gleawceastre. & þær bebyrged. "[('', '1104.')]",Her on þisum geare to Cristes mæssan heold se cyng Heanrig his hired æt Wæstminstre. & to Eastron on Winceastre. & to Pentecosten eft on Westmynstre. "[('', '1104.')]",Ðises geares wæs se forma Pentecostes dæg onNonæ Iunii. "[('', '1104.')]",& on þam Tiwæsdæge þæræfter ætywdan feower circulas to þam mid dæge onbutan þære sunnan hwites hiwes. ælc under oðran gebroiden. swylce hi gemette wæron. "[('', '1104.')]",Ealle þe hit gesawon wundredon. forþan hi næfre ær swilce ne gemundon. "[('', '1104.')]",Heræfter wurdon sehte se eorl Rotbert of Normandig. & Rotbert de Bælesme þe se cyng Heanri æror belænd hæfde & of Englalande adrifen. "[('', '1104.')]",& þurh heora sehte wurdon wiðerræde se cyng of Englalande & se eorl of Normandig. "[('', '1104.')]",& se cyng his folc ofer sæ into Normandig sende. & þa heafodmen þær on lande hi underfengon. "[('', '1104.')]",& on heora hlafordes þæs eorles swicdome into heora castelan gelogodan. þanon hi manige gedrecednissa on hergunga & on bærninge þam eorle gedydon. "[('', '1104.')]",Eac þises geares Willelm eorl of Moretoin heonon of lande into Normandig for. "[('', '1104.')]",Ac syððan he afaren wes. he wið þone cyng geworhte. for hwan hine se cyng ealles benæmde. & belænde þæs þe he her on lande hæfde. "[('', '1104.')]",Nis eaðe to asecgenne þises landes earmða þe hit to þysan timan dreogende wæs. þurh mistlice & mænigfealdlice unriht & gyld. þæ næfre ne geswican ne ne ateorodon. "[('', '1104.')]",& æfre ealswa se cyng for. full hergung þurh his hired uppon his wreccea folc wæs. & þær onmang foroft bærneta. & manslihtas. "[('', '1104.')]",Eall þis wæs God mid to gremienne. & þas arme leode mid to tregienne. "[('', '1105.')]",On þisum geare to Natiuiteð heold se cyng Heanrig his hired æt Windlesoran. "[('', '1105.')]",& þæræfter to þam lengtene he for ofer sæ into Normandig uppon his broðer Rotbert eorl. "[('', '1105.')]",& onmang þam þe he þær wunode he gewann of his broðer Caþum & Baius. & mæst ealle þa castelas & þa heafodmen þær on lande him wurdon underþeodde. & se syððan to herfest eft ongean hider to lande com. "[('', '1105.')]",& þæt he on Normandig gewunnen hæfde. syððan on sibbe & him gebygle wunode. butan þa þe þam eorle Willelme of Mortoin ahwær neah wunedon. þa he gelomlice geswæncte swa he swiðost mihte. for his landlyre her on lande. "[('', '1105.')]",And þa toforan Cristes mæssan com Rotbert de Bælesme hider to lande to þam cynge. "[('', '1105.')]",Ðis wæs swiðe gedyrfsum gear her on lande þurh wæstma forwordenessa. & þurh þa mænigfealde gyld þe næfre ne geswican ær se cyng oferfore. & þa hwile þe he þær wæs. & eft syððan he ongean com. "[('', '1106.')]",Her on þison geare wæs se cyng Henrig to Natiuiteð on Westmynstre. & þær his hired heold. "[('', '1106.')]",& uppon þære tide Rotbert de Bælesme mid unsehte fram þam cynge ut of þison lande into Normandige for. "[('', '1106.')]",Ða her æfter onforan længtene wæs se cyng æt Norðhamtune. & se eorl Rotbert his broðer of Normandig þyder to him com. "[('', '1106.')]",& forþam se cyng him nolde agifan þæt þe he on Normandige uppon him genumen hæfde. hi mid unsehte tohwurfon. & se eorl ferde ofer s [[../images/etail.gif]]sona eft ongean. "[('', '1106.')]",On þære forman længtenwucan on þone Frigedægi xiiii kalendæ Marciion æfen ætywde an ungewunelic steorra. & lange stunde þæræfter wæs ælce æfen gesewen hwile scinende. "[('', '1106.')]",Se steorra ætywde innon þæt suðwest. he wæs litel geþuht. and deorc. ac se leoma þe him fram stod wæs swiðe beorht. & swilce ormæte beam geþuht norðeast scinende. "[('', '1106.')]",& sumne æfen wæs gesæwen swilce se beam ongeanweardes wið þes steorran ward fyrcliende wære. "[('', '1106.')]",Gehwylce sædon þæt hig ma on þison timon uncuðra steorra gesawon. ac we hit openlicor ne awriton. forþam þe we hit sylfe ne sawon. "[('', '1106.')]",On þa niht þe on morgen wæsCena Domini. þæt is se þunresdæg toforan Eastran. wæron gesewen twegen monan on þære heofonan toforan þam dæge oðer beeastan. & se oðer be westan begen fulle. & þæs ylcan dæges wæs se monaxiiii. "[('', '1106.')]",To Eastran wæs se cyng æt Baðan. & to Pentecosten æt Searbyrig. forþam þe he nolde on his fundunge ofer sæ hired healdan. "[('', '1106.')]",Ðæræfter toforan August ferde se cyng ofer sæ into Normandig. & ealle mæst þe þær on lande wæron him on his willan to gebugon. wiðuton Rotbert de Bælesme. & þam eorle of Moretoin. & feawa oðre of þam heafodmannan þe mid þam eorle of Normandige þe gyt heoldan. "[('', '1106.')]",& forþan se cyng syððan mid fyrde for. & besæt þæs eorles ænne castel of Moretoin Tenercebrai hatte. "[('', '1106.')]",Onmang þam þe se cyng þone castel besæt. com se eorl Rotbert of Normandig on sancte Michaeles mæsseæfen uppon þone cyng mid his fyrde. & mid him Rotbert de Bælesme. & Willelm eorl of Moretoin. & ealle þa þe mid heom woldan. "[('', '1106.')]",Ac seo streongðe & se sige wearð þæs cynges. "[('', '1106.')]",Ðær wearð se eorl of Normandig gefangen. & se eorl of Moretoin. & Rotbert de Stutteuile. & to Englalande syððan gesende. & on hæftneðe gebrohte. "[('', '1106.')]",Rotbert de Bælesme þær wearð aflymed. & Willelm Crispin gelæht. & manige forð mid. "[('', '1106.')]",Eadgar æþeling þe litle ær fram þam cynge to þam eorle wæs gefaren þær wæs eac gefangen. þone let se cyng syððan sacleas faran. "[('', '1106.')]",Syððan geeode se cyng eall þæt on Normandige wæs. & hit on his willan & geweald gesette. "[('', '1106.')]",Ðises geares eac wæron swiðe hefige & sinlice gewinn betwux þam Casere of Sexlande & his sunu. & onmang þam gewinnan se fæder forðferde. & se sunu feng to þam rice. "[('', '1107.')]",On þisum geare to Cristes mæssan wæs se cyng Henri on Normandig. & þæt land on his geweald dihte. & sette. "[('', '1107.')]",& þæræfter to længtene hider to lande com. & to Eastran his hired on Windlesoran heold. & to Pentecosten on Westminstre. "[('', '1107.')]",& syððan eft to Augustes anginne on Westmynstre wæs. & þær þa biscopricen & geaf. & sette. þe on Englelande oððe on Normandige buton ealdre & hyrde . "[('', '1107.')]",Ðera wæron swa fela swa nan man næs þe gemvnde þæt æfre ær swa fela togædere gyfene wæron. "[('', '1107.')]",& æt þes ylcan syðe. onmang þa oððre þe abbodrices underfengon. Ernulf þe ær wæs prior on Cantwarbyrig feng to þam abbodrice on Burh. "[('', '1107.')]",Ðis wæs rihtlice ymbeviigear þæs þe se cyng Henri cynedomes onfeng. & wæs þæt an and fowertigeðe gear þæs þe Francan þyses landes weoldan. "[('', '1107.')]",Manege sædon þet hi on þam monan þyses geares mistlice tacna gesawon. & ongean cynde his leoman wexende & waniende. "[('', '1107.')]",Ðises geares forðferdon. Mauricius biscop on Lunden. & Rotbert abbod on sancte Eadmundes byrig. & Ricard abbod on Elig. "[('', '1107.')]",Ðises geares eac forðferde se cyng Eadgar on ScotlandeIDus Ianuarii. & feng Alexander his broðer to þam rice swa se cyng Henri him geuðe. "[('', '1108.')]",Her on þisum geare wes se cyng Henri to Natiuiteð on Westmynstre. & to Eastron on Winceastre. & to Pentecosten eft on Westmynstre. & þæræfter toforan Augusti he ferde into Normandig. "[('', '1108.')]",& se cyng of France Philippus forðferdeNonæ Augusti. & feng his sunu Loðewis to þam rice. "[('', '1108.')]",& wurdon syððon manege gewinn betwux þam cynge of France & þam of Englelande. þa hwile þe he on Normandig wunode. "[('', '1108.')]",On þisum geare eac forðferde se arcebiscop Girard of Eoferwic toforan Pentecosten. & wearð syððan Thomas þærto gesett. "[('', '1109.')]",Her on þison geare wæs se cyng Henri to Cristes mæssan & to Eastron on Normandig. & toforan Pentecosten hider to lande com. & his hired on Westmynstre heold. "[('', '1109.')]",Ðær wurdon þa forewearda fullworhte. & þa aðas gesworene his dohter þam Casere to gifene. "[('', '1109.')]",Ðises geares gewurdon swiðe fela þunra. & þa swiðe ægeslice. "[('', '1109.')]",And se arcebiscop Ansealm of Cantwarabyrig forðferde on þam dægexi kalendæ Aprilis. & wæs se forma Easterdæg onLetania maior. "[('', '1110.')]",On þisum geare heold se cyng Henri his hired to Cristesmæssan æt Westmynstre. & to Eastron he wæs æt Mærlebeorge. & to Pentecosten forman siþe his hired on þam niwan Windlesoran heold. "[('', '1110.')]",Ðises geares sende se cyng toforan længtene his dohter mid mænigfealdan madman ofer sæ. & hi þam Casere forgeaf. "[('', '1110.')]",On þære fiftan nihte on Maies monðe. ætywde se mona on æfen beorhte scinende. & syððan litlan & litlan his leoht wanode. swa þæt he sona nihtes to þam swiðe mid ealle acwanc. þæt naþer ne leoht ne trændel ne nan þing mid ealle of him wæs gesæwen. "[('', '1110.')]",& swa þurhwunode fullneah oð dæg. & syðþan full & beorhte scinende ætywde. he wæs þæs ylcan dæges feowertyne nihta eald. "[('', '1110.')]",Ealle þa niht wæs seo lyft swiðe clene. & þa steorran ofer eall þa heofon swiðe beorhte scinende. & treowwæstmas wurdon þære nihte þurh forste swiðe fornumene. "[('', '1110.')]",Ðær æfter on Iunies monðe ætywde an steorra norðaneastan. & his leoma stod toforan him on þet suðwest. & þus manega niht wæs gesæwen. "[('', '1110.')]",& furðor nihtes syððan he ufor astah. he wæs gesewen onbæc on þæt norðwest gangende. "[('', '1110.')]",Ðises geares wurdon belænde Philippus de Brause. & Willelm Mallet. & Willelm Bainart. "[('', '1110.')]",Eac þises geares forðferde Elias eorl. þe þa Mannie of þam cynge Heanri geheold. & on cweow. "[('', '1110.')]",& æfter his forsiðe feng to se eorl of Angeow. & hi togeanes þam cynge heold. "[('', '1110.')]",Ðis wæs swiðe gedeorfsum gear her on lande þurh gyld þe se cyng nam for his dohter gyfte. & þurh ungewædera. for hwan eorðwestmas wurdon swiðe amyrde. & treowwestmas ofer eall þis land forneah eall forwurdon. "[('', '1110.')]",Ðises geares me began ærost to weorcenne on þam niwan mynstre on Ceortesæge. "[('', '1111.')]",On þison geare ne bær se kyng Henri his coronan to Cristes mæssan. ne to Eastron. ne to Pentecosten. "[('', '1111.')]",& innan August he ferde ofer sæ into Normandig. for unsehte þe wið him hæfdon sume be þam gemæran of France. & swiðost for þam eorle of Angeow þe þa Mannie togeanes him heold. "[('', '1111.')]",And syððan he þyder ofer com. manega unrada & bærnetta & hergunga hi heom betweonan gedydan. "[('', '1111.')]",On þison geare forðferde se eorl Rotbert of Flandran. & feng his sunu Baldewine þærto. "[('', '1111.')]",Ðises geares wæs swiðe lang winter. & hefig tyme. & strang. & þurh þæt eorðwæstmas wurdon swiðe amyrde. & gewearð se mæsta orfcwealm þe ænig mann mihte gemunan. "[('', '1112.')]",Eall þis gear wunode se cyng Henri on Normandig for þære unsehte þe he hæfde wið France. & wið þone eorl of Angeow þe þa Mannie togeanes him heold. "[('', '1112.')]",& onmang þam þe he þær wæs. he belænde þone eorl of Eureus. & Willelm Crispin. & ut of Normandi adraf. "[('', '1112.')]",& Philippe de Braus his land ageaf. þe ær wæs belænd. & Rotbert de Bælesme he let niman & on prisune don. "[('', '1112.')]",Ðis wæs swiðe god gear & swiðe wistfull on wudan & on feldan. ac hit wæs swiðe hefig tyme & sorhfull þurh ormætne mancwealm. "[('', '1113.')]",Her on þison gear wæs se cyng Henri to Natiuiteð & to Eastron. & to Pentecosten on Normandig. "[('', '1113.')]",& þæræfter to sumeran he sænde hider to lande Rotbert de Bælesme into þam castele to Wærham. & himsylf sona þæræfter hider to lande com. "[('', '1114.')]",On þison geare heold se cyng Henri his hyred to Natiuiteð on Windlesoran. & þær geares syððan he ne heold hired nan oftar. "[('', '1114.')]",And tomiddan sumeran he ferde mid fyrde into Wealon. & þa Wyliscean coman & wið þone cyng griðedon. "[('', '1114.')]",& he let þær inne castelas weorcean. & þæræfter innan Septembris he for ofer sæ into Normandig. "[('', '1114.')]",Ðises geares on æfteward Mai wæs gesewen an selcuð steorra mid langan leoman manege niht scinende. "[('', '1114.')]",Eac on þis ylcan geare wæs swa mycel ebba æghwær anes dæges swa nan man æror ne gemunde. & swa þæt man ferde ridende & gangende ofer Tæmese be eastan þære brigge on Lunden. "[('', '1114.')]",Þises geares wæron swiðe mycele windas on Octobris monðe. ac he wæs ormæte mycel on þa niht Octabris sancti Martini. & þæt gehwær on wudan & on tunan gecydde. "[('', '1114.')]",Eac on þisum geare se cyng geaf þet on Cantwarabyrig Raulfe. se wæs æror biscop on Hrofeceastre. "[('', '1114.')]",And se arcebiscop on Eoferwic Thomas forðferde. & feng Turstein þærto. se wæs æror þæs cynges capelein. "[('', '1114.')]",On þæs ylcan tyme feorde se cyng toweard þone sæ & ofer wolde. ac wæder him lætte. "[('', '1114.')]",Þa hwile þa sende he his writ æfter þone abbod Ernulf of Burh. & bebead him þæt he efeostlice scolde to him cuman. forþi þæt he wolde sprecon mid him dærne sprece. "[('', '1114.')]",Ða he to him com. þa neodde he him to þam biscoprice of Hrofeceastre. & þa arcebiscopes & biscopes & þæt dugeð þæt wæs on Englalande forð mid se cyng. "[('', '1114.')]",& he lange wiðstod. ac hit ne forheol naht. "[('', '1114.')]",& se cyng þa bebead þone arcebiscop þæt he sceolde him læden to Cantwarabyrig & blætson him to biscop wolde he nolde he. "[('', '1114.')]",Þis wæs don on þære tuna þa man cleopað Burne. þæt wæs þes dægesxvii kalendæ Octobris. "[('', '1114.')]",Ða þe munecas of Burch hit herdon sægen. þa wæron hi swa sari swa hi næfre ær ne wæron. forþi þæt he wæs swiðe god & softe man. & dyde mycel to gode wiðinnan & wiðutan. þa hwile þe he þær wunode. "[('', '1114.')]",God ælmihtig wunie æfre mid him. "[('', '1114.')]",Ða sona þæræfter þa geaf se cyng þone an munec of Sæis Iohan wæs gehaten. þurh þæs gearnunge of Cantwarbyrig. "[('', '1114.')]",& sona þæræfter sende se cyng him & se of to Rome æfter þes <ærcebiscopes> pallium. & an munec mid him Warner is gehaten. & þone ærcediæcne Iohane þes arcebiscop neafe. & hi þær wellspæddon. "[('', '1114.')]","Ðis wæs don þes dægesxi kalendæ Octobris, on þone tuna þe man cleopað Rugenore." "[('', '1114.')]",& þes ylces dæges eode se cyng on scipa on Portesmuðe. "[('', '1115.')]",Her wæs se cyng Henri to Natiuiteð on Normandig. & onmang þam þe he þær wæs. he dyde þæt ealle þa heafodmæn on Normandig dydon manræden & holdaðas his sunu Willelme þe he be his cwene hæfde. "[('', '1115.')]",& æfter þan syððan innon Iulies monðe hider into lande com. "[('', '1115.')]",Ðises geares wæs swa strang winter mid snawe & mid forste. swa nan man þe þa lifode ær þan nan strengre ne gemunde. & wearð þurh þæt ungemæte orfcwealm. "[('', '1115.')]",On þison geare sænde se papa Paschalis Raulfe <ærcebiscop> on Cantwarabyrig pallium hider to lande. & he his onfeng mid mycelan wurðscipe æt his arcestole on Cantwarabyrig. "[('', '1115.')]",Hine brohte Ansealm abbod of Rome se wæs nefa Ansealmes ærcebiscop. & se abbod Iohan of Burh. "[('', '1116.')]",On þison geare wæs se cyng Henri to Natiuiteð æt sancte Albane. & þær let þæt mynster halgian. & to Eastron on Wudiham. "[('', '1116.')]",& Wes eac þyses geares swiðe hefigtyme winter & strang & lang. wið orf & wið ealle þing. "[('', '1116.')]",And se cyng æfter Eastron sona ferde ofer sæ into Normandig. & wurdon manega unrada & ræfunga. & castelas genumene betwux France & Normandig. "[('', '1116.')]",Mæst þis unsehte wæs forþan þe se cyng Henri fylste his nefan þam eorle Tædbalde de Blais. þe þa wyrre hæfde togeanes his hlaforde þam cynge of France Loðewis. "[('', '1116.')]",Ðis wæs swiðe geswincfull gear & byrstfull on eorðwæstman. þurh þa ormæte reinas þe coman sona onforan August. & swiðe gedrehton & geswencton þe gyt þe com Candelmæssan. "[('', '1116.')]",Eac þis gear wæs swa gæsne on mæstene. swa þæt on eallon þison lande. ne eac on Wealon ne gehyrde me of nanan segcean. "[('', '1116.')]",Ðis land & þas leodon wurdon eac þyses geares oftrædlice sare geswencte. þurh þa gyld þe se cyng nam. ægðer ge binnan burgan & butan. "[('', '1116.')]",On þisum ylcan geare bærnde eall þæt mynstre of Burh. & eallæ þa husas butan se Captelhus & se Slæpperne. & þær to eac bærnde eall þa mæste dæl of þa tuna. "[('', '1116.')]",Eall þis belamp on an Frigdæg. þæt wæsii Nonæ Augusti. "[('', '1117.')]",Eall þis gear wunode se cyng Henri on Normandig. for þes cynges unsehte of France & his oðra nehhebura. "[('', '1117.')]",& þa to ðan sumeran com se cyng of France & se eorl of Flandra mid him mid fyrde into Normandig. & ane niht þærinne wunedon. & on morgen butan gefeohte ongean ferden. "[('', '1117.')]",& Normandig wearð swiðe gedreht. ægðer ge þurh gyld. ge þurh fyrde þe se cing Henri þær ongean gaderode. "[('', '1117.')]",Eac þeos þeode þurh þis ylce þurh manigfealde gyld. wearð strange geswenct. "[('', '1117.')]",Eac on þære nihtexvii kalendæ Ianuariiwæs seo heofon swyðe read gesewen. swylce hit bryne wære.
